This time, the dignitaries came to Lushan to visit Jiang without any formal meetings, just to discuss national affairs. Presidents Sun and Wang and President Kong have all set off to Jiangxi, etc. At around 1:00 PM, Song and others took several cars and drove from Xun to Lianhua Cave, where they transferred to sedan chairs to Guling. They arrived at Jiang at around 3:00 PM. Jiang and Song met very happily. That night, Song had a long talk with Jiang at Jiang's private residence, reporting on his attendance at the economic conference and his visits to various countries. They made preliminary consultations on domestic and foreign policy issues. As soon as Wang, Sun, Kong, and others arrive in Lushan one after another, a meeting will be held to exchange opinions. It is also heard that if all the participants can arrive on the fifth day, the meeting will officially open on the sixth day. It is heard that the main cases to be discussed are: 1) The plan to develop the national economy and enrich the people's livelihood and national power; 2) The new diplomatic approach; 3) The plan for the distribution of American wheat and cotton loans; 4) Central fiscal issues; 5) National defense construction; 6) All control policies to cope with the national crisis; 7) The implementation plan for technical cooperation with the League of Nations; and the post-disaster recovery in North China and the Yellow River flood relief. It is heard that after Song has a complete plan, he will take it back to Nanjing and submit it to the central government for approval and implementation. (September 5)

Diary of an Inspection of the Northwest Frontier (2) Feng Youzhen

Lanzhou Correspondence: Luo Junwu, Minister of Foreign Affairs and Minister of Justice and Administration, was ordered to inspect Xinjiang. The reporter has already reported that Luo has arrived in Xi'an. Now, Luo has arrived in Lanzhou yesterday (29th) and will fly to Xinjiang tomorrow (31st). I will describe the past few days as follows.

(8) Oppressive Continuous Rain

On August 27th, it rained as soon as it dawned. Although it stopped temporarily, the overcast sky did not dissipate, showing no signs of clearing. It was known that the 8 AM flight plan would be difficult to realize again. Indeed, the air station reported that the weather was bad and it was decided that they could not fly, which was truly frustrating. After breakfast, I went to visit Wolong Temple. The temple was built during the reign of Emperor Taizong of the Tang Dynasty. The Buddha statues and sculptures in the temple are extremely exquisite, enough to represent Eastern art. In the overcast rain, the Buddha's head drooped slightly forward, probably due to the wooden material, but it was also amazing. The temple has a very rich collection of scriptures, but they were stolen and transported by the bandit Kang Sheng during the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, and the essence was lost. Chairman Lin and Dean Dai stayed at the temple during their previous visit to Shaanxi. It is indeed a holy place for cultivating the mind. Then I went to the Confucian Temple. The temple is quite magnificent, especially the towering ancient trees, all of which are hundreds or even thousands of years old, making it rare to see. I returned to my residence at ten o'clock. It rained again in the afternoon, and I was confined indoors and did not go out. Only the President of the Local Court came to visit Minister Luo and presented a prison report. At six o'clock, Mr. Qiu Yuanwu, the president of the Xijing Daily, personally invited me to dinner. We took a donkey cart to the Northwest Hotel. The donkey cart is the only effective transportation tool in the north, but it is clumsy and unbearable. It bumps and sways during travel, making people feel like their livers and guts are about to break. It is not something that southerners are accustomed to. A strange thing happened in the Northwest Hotel today, that is, a hen laid an egg. I saw it myself. The egg was small like a ginkgo, with a dull yellow color. What was previously considered heresy is now undeniable. After returning to my residence, I read various reference documents and went to bed at midnight. On the 28th, the sky was still overcast and then continuous rain. The air station reported that the weather in Lanzhou was even worse than here, so I had to stay indoors for another day. In the afternoon, Chairman Shao and Chairman Yang Ren both came to visit Minister Luo.

The issue of developing the South and opening up the Northwest has been around for a long time.

(9) Taking off for Lanzhou

On the 29th, the rain stopped and the clouds cleared, and the sun filled the sky. It was decided to take off for Lanzhou at 9:30 AM. At 8 AM, Shao and Yang Ren both came to visit Minister Luo and continued to discuss the issue of developing the Northwest for an hour. At 9 AM, I took a car to the airport. The military and political leaders of the provincial capital, as well as the national officers and soldiers of the Special Service Regiment and the military band, gave a warm send-off at the airport. At 9:40 AM, the plane flew westward. In about an hour, we reached Liupan Mountain. The peaks and ridges were piled up like camps, winding and endless, and beautifully verdant. After passing Liupan Mountain, it was all bare, barren, and glaringly desolate. We encountered heavy fog on the way. The plane traveled bumpy and uneven, and it was extremely dangerous. Minister Luo vomited heavily because of this. Fortunately, the pilot was skilled and we arrived safely in Lanzhou.

(10) Welcoming Ten Li Outside the City

The Lanzhou airport is about twelve li from the city. All sectors have been looking forward to Minister Luo's arrival and have been going back and forth to welcome him for three days. At 12:30 PM, the plane landed safely. Lanzhou time was 11:30 AM, exactly one hour later than Xi'an time. Those welcoming at the airport included Zhu Shaoliang, Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government; Deng Baoshan, Pacification Director; Ma Lin, Chairman of the Qinghai Provincial Government, who had just arrived in Gansu two days ago; Shui Zi, Director of the Gansu Provincial Education Department; Liu Ruban, Director of the Construction Department; Tan Kemin, Director of the Finance Department; Wei Fuzi, Director of the Civil Affairs Department; Li Zhengzhong, Secretary-General; Ma Weiliang, Garrison Commander of the Linxia District; Zeng Youhao, President of the High Court; Zhan Shiming, Chief Prosecutor; Ling Zixing and Zhang Wenwei of the Provincial Party Committee; Cao Qiwu of the Xinjiang Provincial Party Committee; Hui leaders Ma Guoli and Ma Guodong; representatives from various agencies, schools, and mass organizations; and about two to three thousand military police. Minister Luo got off the plane amidst the music and applause of the military band, feeling dizzy. He shook hands with each of the welcoming personnel as a courtesy. After passing through the welcoming arch, he entered the city in the same car as Chairman Zhu and Chairman Ma. The enthusiasm of the border province people in supporting the central government could be seen here.

(10)(1) Provincial Government Banquet

Minister Luo stayed at the Provincial Government, which was formerly the Prince Su Mansion and then the Gansu-Shaanxi Governor's Mansion during the Qing Dynasty. It is extremely spacious, with a garden in the rear, leading directly to the edge of the city. Outside the city is the turbulent Yellow River. After arriving at the Provincial Government, we rested briefly and then had lunch. All the military and political leaders accompanied us. After the meal, we toured the Provincial Government's garden and climbed the Yellow Crane Tower for a panoramic view. The entire city was clearly visible. The city of Lanzhou is about ten li in circumference, two li from north to south, and seven li from east to west. Gaolan Mountain surrounds the area, and the Yellow River flows under the city. The terrain is dangerous and unparalleled. After two o'clock, Minister Luo and I went to the High Court, the Local Court, the First Prison, and the Detention Center for inspection. Zeng Youhao, President of the High Court, explained everything in detail, and Minister Luo also inquired and gave many instructions. Then we paid return visits to various important military and political leaders. At six o'clock, Chairman Zhu of the Provincial Government hosted a formal banquet, and everyone dispersed in joy. In the evening, Minister Luo and Chairman Zhu discussed the issue of developing the Northwest, and they hit it off. They talked for two or three hours before going to bed late at night. Minister Luo originally planned to fly to Hami tomorrow (30th), but due to the earnest requests from all sectors, it was decided to hold a welcome meeting tomorrow morning. The purpose of Ma Lin, Ma Weiliang, etc., is to hope that Minister Luo will stop and inspect when passing through Liangzhou and Ganzhou, so the departure date has to be postponed for one day, and the time required has to be increased slightly.

(10)(2) Gansu Province Justice

The situation of justice in Gansu Province can be summarized as follows: (1) Financial difficulties. Since the Northwest Army arrived in Gansu in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, due to the heavy military expenses, judicial personnel only received a maintenance fee of 20 yuan per month. Gradually, only 30 to 40 percent of that was paid. The staff worked for the public service on an empty stomach and were extremely distressed. Last year, the Provincial Government was officially established, and funding increased slightly, but it still appeared to be depleted from time to time. The President of the High Court only received a maintenance fee of 80 yuan per month, the Chief Prosecutor 70 yuan, the Clerk 50 yuan, and the Recording Secretary only 10 yuan. Even this small amount could not be paid in full every month. (2) Court organization. The High Court is located in the provincial capital, and branch courts are established in Liangzhou, Tianshui, Suzhou, and Pingliang. The Gaolan Local Court is established, and judicial offices are established in 34 counties including Lintao, Linxia, Lintan, and Minxian. The county magistrate concurrently serves as the prosecutor, and each office has one judge. The judiciary in the remaining counties is handled concurrently by the county magistrate. As for prisons, the First Prison in the provincial capital has been established, and the Second Prison in Liangzhou. New prisons have also been built in Tianshui, Pingliang, and Suzhou one after another, but either due to lack of funds for operation, they have been damaged by the stationed troops after completion, or due to insufficient construction funds, they have been abandoned halfway and have no ability to continue repairs, resulting in the abandonment of all efforts, which is very regrettable. (3) There are not many lawsuits, and the court has no backlog. The High Court handles about two to three civil appeal cases, three to four third-instance cases, two to three appeals, and eight to nine miscellaneous cases each month. The criminal appeal cases number about three to four, the criminal third-instance cases two to three, the review cases two to three, and the banditry cases one to two. In terms of the nature of the lawsuits, criminal cases are mostly homicide and theft cases. This is probably due to the strong character of the people. Civil cases concerning debt are at most only one or two thousand yuan. This shows the suffering of the people in the Northwest. Cases of fraud, enticement, and divorce, which are common in the southern provinces, are almost non-existent. Browsing through the files, I only saw one woman who, because her husband had been away for a long time and she was forced by livelihood, requested the court to allow her to remarry. This is completely different in nature from divorce cases in the South.

(10)(3) Warm Welcome

In Gansu Province, all sectors have decided to hold a welcome meeting at 9 AM on the 30th to express their warm welcome to Minister Luo and Ma Lin, Chairman of the Qinghai Provincial Government, who have arrived in Gansu one after another. Minister Luo could not refuse, so he had to stay one more day. On the 30th, the weather was clear. At 7 AM, the Guangdong fellow villagers in Gansu held a tea party to welcome Minister Luo. There were about twenty Guangdong people in Gansu, mostly engaged in the watch and photography business. Recalling the time in Xi'an, I learned that the watch and photography industry in Xi'an was also dominated by Guangdong people. Is this a specialty of Guangdong people? At 9 AM, I attended the welcome meeting. The meeting place was the square outside the gate of the Provincial Government. There was a building on the square, which was a natural rostrum. Those who participated in the welcome meeting included more than ten thousand people from party, government, military, police, various mass organizations, and schools. Their enthusiastic and sincere emotions were incomparable to the superficial welcome meetings in the South. Here, one could see the enthusiasm of the border people in supporting the central government and their eagerness to hope that the central government would save the people from suffering. After the meeting began as scheduled, Zhu Shaoliang, the chairman, delivered the opening speech.

Page 12

Followed by speeches from Minister Luo, Chairman Ma, Li Dan, a member of the Supervisory Committee residing in Gansu, and Deng Baoshan, the Pacification Director. All unanimously expressed their sincere support for the central government and their gratitude to the central government for caring about the border areas. They especially hoped that the central government would start developing the Northwest. The meeting adjourned at 10:30 AM. Minister Luo then went to the High Court to attend the welcome meeting of the judicial community of the entire city and delivered a speech. At noon, the legal community welcomed him for more than an hour before returning to his residence to rest. At 3 PM, the preparatory committee for the welcome meeting from all sectors held a concert at the Education Center. I had the opportunity to listen to Qinqiang opera. Although I was ignorant of the meaning, the impassioned and tragic songs and the激昂tone were clearly different from the靡靡之音 in the South. At 6 PM, all sectors held a banquet, with more than a hundred people attending. At 8 PM, I returned to the Provincial Government and received a telegram from Chairman Chiang. Ma Bufang, commander of the 9th Division of Qinghai, and Ma Buqing, commander of the 2nd Cavalry Division of Liangzhou, also sent telegrams. Mr. Ma Buqing also strongly requested Minister Luo to stay in Liangzhou for a short visit. It is scheduled to fly to Liangzhou tomorrow (31st), but I don't know what the weather will be like tomorrow morning. The plane that flew out of Xi'an at 5 AM this morning is still missing as of the time of writing. It may have encountered an accident. This section of the flight is extremely dangerous if the weather is not good.

(10)(4) Impressions of Lanzhou

I have been staying in Lanzhou for two days, busy with social events, and there is no time to spare. Although the enthusiasm of all parties is appreciable, I am ultimately disappointed that I have not been able to see the social conditions of Lanzhou. The city of Lan is surrounded by mountains on all sides and faces the river on one side. The terrain is extremely dangerous. The streets are narrow and uneven. On the surface, it seems inferior to Xi'an, but in reality, it is even worse. It is said that the climate here is excellent. The hottest in summer is no more than eighty-two or three degrees, and the winter is not as cold as Nanjing. It is only slightly dry. The land is extremely fertile. The melons, fruits, and vegetables that are produced in Jiangzhe are all produced here, and they are much larger and more fertile. However, water conservancy is not well-maintained, and farmers rely entirely on the weather. If the rainfall is harmonious, the yield of one year is enough for three years, but if the weather is not suitable, they are helpless. Gansu Province is rich in products. Medicinal materials occupy the most important position in the country, and wool is also a major product. Coal oil is readily available in the Yumen area. There are many other things that cannot be mentioned. Unfortunately, due to traffic obstruction and inconvenient transportation, the goods needed by this province from other provinces are also extremely expensive due to inconvenient transportation. Now, let's give an example: Meili brand cigarettes, which can be purchased for two yuan per can in Beijing and Shanghai, cost two yuan per can here. The value of other goods is four or five times higher. The transportation in Gansu Province relies on donkey carts on land and oxhide rafts on the water. Oxhide rafts are made of six or seven or more than ten whole cowhides, stuffed with wool, and connected to form a raft that can float on the water. It flows downstream and is quite fast. All goods transported from Gansu to Sui rely on this as a sharp tool, but it cannot go upstream. Therefore, after arriving in Sui, it is dismantled and carried back to Gansu. Such is the endless cycle. Therefore, what the people of the Northwest expect from the central government's development of the Northwest does not require grand plans. Their only hope is to develop transportation. The first hope is to complete the Longhai Railway, and the second is to complete the various highways. If the roads are smooth, transportation will be convenient, and if water conservancy can be further improved, the people of the Northwest will not have to worry about freezing and starvation, and prosperity can be expected. If it is not developed, it will develop itself. (August 30, sent from Lanzhou)

North China Compatriots Mourn the National Tragedy Together

He Yingqin and Huang Shaohong Preside Over the Memorial Service; Relatives of the Martyrs Cry Bitterly at the Venue

Beiping Special Dispatch: The North China Anti-Japanese War Martyrs Conference, organized by the Beiping Military Branch, held a public memorial service at the Tianwang Hall of Beihai Park, starting at 9 AM on the 4th and ending at 6 PM. At 8 PM, a Dharma boat was burned. More than ten thousand Chinese and foreign people attended the memorial service. He Yingqin, Acting Chairman of the Military Branch, presided over the memorial service on behalf of Chiang Kai-shek. Huang Shaohong, Minister of the Interior, presided over the memorial service on behalf of Wang Zhaoming. Zhao Shuyong, a member of the Political Consolidation Committee, participated in the memorial service on behalf of Huang Fu. In addition to preparing all the memorial rituals, the association also invited monks from Guangji Temple, Taoists from Baiyun Temple, and Lamas from Yonghe Palace to chant scriptures, and made large paper Dharma boats and towers to transcend the dead souls. In addition, the 67th Army Headquarters originally planned to hold a memorial service for the Anti-Japanese War Martyrs of the 67th Army on July 2nd at the Langfang defense line. It has notified all parties and invited them to participate in the memorial service. As a result, Beijing merged with the Beiping conference. All the elegiac couplets sent by various parties that the army received, more than ten pieces, were sent to the conference by the adjutant Tong to be hung up. The situation of the memorial service is recorded as follows:

Arrangement and Vigilance

Plain-colored arches were built in front of and outside the North Sea Gate and the Tianwang Hall. The hall was covered with mourning couplets and wreaths. Lamas, Taoists, and monks chanted scriptures in the east, west, and south. The band played mourning music with the memorial service. The portrait of the Prime Minister was hung high in the hall, with the party and national flags crossed. Below were the tablets and portraits of the martyrs. Small flags were inserted between the trees on the road from the back gate of Beihai to the Tianwang Hall, with the words "It is an honor to die for the country." Military police with guns were stationed at each gate and on the roads around the sea. Anyone without an admission pass was not allowed to enter. The arrangements were orderly, and the vigilance was strict.

Situation of the Public Memorial Service

The public memorial service began at 9 AM, presided over by He Yingqin and Huang Shaohong. Among the dignitaries who participated in the public memorial service were Jiang Bocheng, Shang Zhen, Wan Fulin, Qian Dajun, Huang Jie, Xu Tingyao, He Zhuguo, Hu Jiesan, San Shouxin, Wei Yisan, He Jingwu, Gao Guizi, Wang Yizhe, Liu Shifu as Song Zheyuan’s representative, Zhang Zhengfang, Bao Gang, Bao Wenyou, Wu KeRen, Tan Qinglin, Liu Yaowu as Liu Zhi's representative, the 15th Route Army and Bai Ruilin as Ningxia Province representative, Wang Zhengping as Wu Peifu’s representative, and Li Hongwen as Yan Xishan’s representative, who bowed three times to the martyrs. Then, the heads of departments and groups of the Military Branch, and the officers and soldiers of the Seventeenth Army, the Second Division, the Sixty-seventh Army, the Third Regiment of the Gendarmerie, and the Thirty-second Army, successively paid their respects. Starting at 1 PM in the afternoon, the Political Consolidation Committee, represented by Zhao Shuyong on behalf of Huang Fu, paid their respects. Next, the municipal government bureaus and Public Security Bureau Chief Bao Yulin led the district chiefs to pay their respects. Subsequently, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Pinghan Bureau, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, various legal groups, and schools successively paid their respects. At 4:30 PM, Spanish Minister Galide, representing the diplomatic corps, arrived to pay their respects. The Military Branch sent counselors Shen Xi, Wang Weixin, and Zhao Qianchen to be responsible for reception. Among the family members of the martyrs who went to pay their respects were the wife of Jin Dingchen and Jin's children. Mrs. Jin wore a blue cheongsam. When performing the ceremony, she was horrified to see the remains. The old mother of Guan Huangquan, a company commander of the 109th Division, also came to the venue and cried out in grief.

Abstract of Elegiac Couplets

The garden of elegiac couplets was hung all over the corridors and under the canopies of the front and rear halls, totaling thousands. All military and political organs, including Chairman Lin, had offerings. The plaque presented by Chairman Lin was "National Tragedy Forever." Wang Jingwei's couplet was "Come and enjoy the inheritance of the dance, playing iron is still like changing the sun-shooting bow." Chiang Kai-shek's couplet was "The righteousness is as thin as the clouds, defending Tianjin and thinking of the martyrs; the battle achievements are inscribed on bamboo and silk, and the incense is offered to comfort the loyal souls." Xu Yongchang's couplet was "The Longcheng Wanli could not resist the rampant sea bandits, the Gubeikou and Xifengkou were cold, the beacon fires were continuous, the iron horses and golden swords, the comrades competed to rush to the disaster, five thousand sable brocades, who is not a generous man, the Qin clouds, Yan trees, and Wujiang, where is the hometown, the Yingtai White Tower, the autumn wind and autumn rain for recruiting souls." Liu Xiang's couplet was "Smashing the head to resist the powerful 胡, the heroic spirits who died are magnificent rivers and mountains, heartbreaking and painful situation, the soul comes with blood and tears filling the passes and mountains." He Chengjun's couplet was "Martyred for the country in distant borders, regardless of fame or name, all shining heroic spirits for thousands of years, painful comrades in arms leave many regrets, regardless of the early or late death, together vent their grief and indignation this morning."

Ronin Want to Worship

Xu Yingtan, director of the memorial service preparatory committee, said that the preparations were rushed and there were many shortcomings. It was originally scheduled to be held for three days, but it was changed to one day after a meeting decision. The budget was set at 5,000 yuan. Since it has been changed to one day, it may be saved. The tablets and portraits of the martyrs supplied are all officials, totaling more than 5,000. There are as many as 10,000 elegiac couplets and wreaths, which shows that the hearts of the people have not died. As for the Beihai gate today, the security is very strict. A ronin from a certain country disguised as a Chinese, trying to force his way into the gate to visit, was discovered by the military police in front of the gate and refused to enter because the ronin had no admission pass. Beihai Park usually burns flower boxes and transports lights on the evening of today (i.e., July 15th of the lunar calendar). The authorities, in consideration of the merchants' difficulties, allowed tickets to be sold as usual at 4 PM this afternoon, allowing people to visit, but visitors are not allowed to enter the Tianwang Hall until the memorial service is over. (Evening of the 4th) Jin

Liu Wenhui's troops are led by Xiang Yuren

Liu's troops still have 30,000 men who have not decided to enter Xikang

Chongqing Correspondence: Since Liu Wenhui left Ya'an, Liu's troops have been led by Xiang Yuren. The military affairs in southern Sichuan have come to an end. What remains to be concluded is the issue of reorganizing the remnant troops of Liu's army on the west bank of the Ya River. Therefore, Liu Xiang's and Deng Xihou's troops are still preparing to cross the river to urge Liu's troops to submit. It is heard that Liu's troops still have about 30,000 men. Liu Wenhui originally wanted to organize all the troops into twenty regiments, with ten regiments stationed in Xikang and ten regiments stationed in Ning District. Later, due to the continued pressure of Liu Deng's troops on the army, and most of the officers and soldiers of the army refused to be stationed in Kang and Ning, and even Kang and Ning were unable to supply this huge military quota, the original proposal was abandoned. The troops stationed in Tianling and Ya'an were handed over to Xiang Yuren for command, so that Xiang could come forward to request Liu Xiang to recruit them, and beg Liu Deng to stop advancing. Liu Wenhui then led his most trusted troops, Liu Wentang, Gao Yucong, Zhu Yinzhou, Qing Hannan, etc., to be stationed in Kang and Ning. There were originally three regiments of Deng Pancun's Brigade stationed in Xikang, and three regiments of Liu Zhulin's troops stationed in Ningyuan. Together with the troops led by Liu Wenhui from Ya'an, there could be sixteen regiments. After Liu left Ya'an, he advanced and stationed in Rongjing, and then moved from Rongjing to Hanyuan. It is heard that he will temporarily stay in Hanyuan or go to Xichang to await the results of Xiang Yuren's request to Liu Xiang. Liu believes that since the troops he leads are limited, it is better to have a foothold in Sichuan than to seek food in other provinces, which is more secure. Liu Zhucun's troops are deploying military forces on the Dadu River, setting up guards along the coast. Liu Wenhui previously sent two regiments to Xichang to help Liu defend it, fearing that after Liu Deng's troops crossed the Ya River, they would thoroughly eliminate the army. Therefore, he dared not rashly retreat into Xikang, because after entering Kang, food and rice must be transported from Ningya to supply military food. If the Luding Bridge is blocked, the troops entering Kang will sit and wait for death. If the counties in Ning are very rich in rice production, and the grain price is low, which is unmatched by other counties in Sichuan, if they retreat to Ning, they will be blockaded by Liu Deng's troops, and the supply will not become a problem. Holding the Dadu River on one side and the Daxiang Ridge on the other, it is enough to defend with danger. If Liu Deng's troops do not advance in the future, Kangning and Rongjing Hanyuan counties can be preserved. It is not too late to enter Kang at this time. Therefore, Liu Wenhui today is still hovering on the wrong path. (September 3rd)

Communist Bandits in Northern Sichuan Are Stirring

Bandits Invading Various Counties of Jiancang Were Repelled; the Bandit Suppression Force Decided to Have 100 Regiments

Chongqing Correspondence: The Red Bandits in northern Sichuan, now that the military affairs of the two Lius have ended, knowing that the Sichuan army will devote all its efforts to suppressing them in the future, and it will be difficult to survive, suddenly attacked Min, Cang, Yi, and Guang counties in an attempt to strike first. Fortunately, the troops of Tian Songyao made every effort to defend them, and the bandits did not succeed and were mostly killed. The situation has been slightly frustrated. Now Liu Xiang has engaged in the allocation of bandit suppression troops, limiting the time to thoroughly clear the bandits. The bandit harm in northern Sichuan and the allocation of bandit suppression troops are detailed as follows:

Xu Xiangqian, the bandit in northern Sichuan, now has more than 30,000 guns and nearly 50,000 to 60,000 people. They are extremely sturdy. Among the communist bandits, he is the strongest except for Zhu De. However, he is cruel by nature and considers killing as his ability. The old are killed, the young are killed, the rich are killed, and the knowledgeable are killed. The established laws for killing are as many as forty-eight kinds, and the tragic situation can be generally seen. Previously, due to a love triangle conflict with Zhang Guoshou (Zhang's cousin Qinqiu and Xu Zhang had private affairs, and the two had been fighting secretly for a long time and would not give in to each other), and the struggle for power, two major camps were formed, and internal strife was quite fierce. Seeing that the Sichuan army was about to launch a large-scale suppression, they launched a large-scale attack on Lang, Cang, Yi, and Guang counties. The troops of Tian Songyao, Liu Hanxiong, and Li Weiru have been advancing one after another to prevent the bandits from advancing, either ten or twenty miles a day, or fifty or sixty miles, step by step. It is heard that the Red Army that departed from Langzhong has reached Puziyan, and the Wang Mingzhang troops have reached Baichipo, the border between Ba and Yi. The bandits have heard the news and retreated to Tong, Nan, Jiangcheng, and the surrounding mountains. The pseudo-division commander Wang Hongmin's troops and the pseudo-28th Regiment Wang's troops and the 31st Regiment, originally stationed in Jiulong, Changle, Longfeng, Zhuguguan, etc., have now gathered in Nanjiang day and night, and it is heard that Xu Xiangqian, Zhang Guoshou, etc., plan to concentrate the main force of the bandits in Changchi, hoping to resist stubbornly. The other key points of Tongnan are guarded by newly organized guerrillas who attack and defend at their discretion. However, the bandit suppression army has stationed heavy troops in Tumen Field, Wei Jialiang, Huanglao Temple, Xinglong Field, Guan Gong Field, and other places, with strict defenses. Although the communist bandits in Yibajie and other places come and go from time to time, they have been repelled by the government army. Now Liu Hanxiong's division has driven the Red Bandits more than thirty miles away from Guang. Seeing that their plan did not succeed, the bandits looted the people's grain on a large scale. The people in the city, seeing their cruelty, wanted to escape. Liu immediately issued a notice explaining that if there were any unforeseen circumstances, he would coexist with Guangcheng and advised the people not to panic and avoid suffering from displacement. The people did not relocate.

As for Liu Xiang's plan to suppress the bandits, he has agreed with Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, Liu Cunhou, etc. He decided to draw bandit suppression troops from each army, temporarily with the regiment as the unit, and a total of 100 regiments will be drawn from the entire Sichuan. Ten airplanes will be added to assist the various armies in suppressing the bandits, and they will be cleared in one fell swoop. (September 1st, Guowen Agency)

Overview of Qingdao Fisheries

The Great Sea Benefits are Seized by Foreigners; The Gains of National Fishermen are Very Small

Qingdao Correspondence: Qing City is located outside the Yellow Sea, with Jiaozhou Bay inside. The bay and harbor are naturally formed, and the islands are lined up. During the spring and autumn seasons, schools of fish migrate and inhabit the nearby sea in abundance. It is truly a great fishing ground on the coast of our country. Unfortunately, most fishermen stick to old methods and do not know how to improve. Therefore, forty years have passed since the port was opened, and various industries have been developing day by day, but the fishing industry has not made progress. Since the third year of the Republic of China, the Japanese occupied Qingdao and vigorously encouraged their fishermen to fish, and established a water production association to handle loan sales and other matters, so that the Qing city fishing industry was manipulated by them. Since the takeover, efforts have been made to rectify it, but due to the frequent changes of government decrees, it has not been possible to actively handle it. Since the Bohai Fleet stationed in Qingdao in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, patrolling and protecting the area and maintaining maritime rights, the fishing industry has begun to improve. After the promotion by the Municipal Social Bureau, wealthy businessmen in the city were persuaded to organize the Qingdao Fisheries Company, which was officially established two years ago. In the past two years, the results have been quite impressive. The overview of the fishing industry is investigated separately as follows:

Fishing Boat Quantities

The residents along the coast of Qingdao and on the various islands, due to the barren land and customary practices, engage in farming for only about one or two tenths of their livelihood, while the rest are engaged in fishing. In 1915, according to a Japanese survey, the Yin Island area had 330 fishing boats and over 1,300 fishermen, with the value of the catch estimated at 25,000 yuan. The Shazikou area had 300 fishing boats and rafts, and over 1,200 fishermen, with the value of the catch estimated at 100,000 yuan. Smaller fishing villages were not included in the statistics. Furthermore, according to a 1926 survey report by the Fisheries and Navigation Bureau, the Qingdao area had over 1,400 fishing boats and 11,000 fishermen. Additionally, around 1917, when the Japanese organized a fisheries association in Qingdao, about 9,200 Chinese fishermen joined. According to recent surveys by the Hebei-Shandong Marine Fisheries Administration and the Qingdao Fisheries Company, Qingdao now has approximately 10,000 fishermen and over 1,400 fishing boats. The fishing areas within the bay are centered around Yin Island, while offshore fishing is centered around Shazikou and Jianggezhuang, extending east beyond Bachidun (Eight Thousand Mounds) to the Q千里島 (Thousand Mile Island), south to Tasu Island and Shuilingshan Island, and to Shidao (Stone Island) within 崂山 (Laoshan) Bay.

Fishermen's Lives

The lives of fishermen, due to the adventurous nature of their work and lack of education, are often dissolute. Most of their hard-earned income is spent on prostitution, gambling, eating, and drinking. Before fishing, all expenses are mostly borrowed from fisheries brokers. After returning with the catch, they sell it to repay the loans. The funds that fisheries brokers lend to fishermen are borrowed from fisheries companies. It is said that fisheries companies provide these interest-free loans, releasing over 60,000 to 70,000 yuan annually. The fishing season is divided into spring and autumn seasons. The spring season is from mid-March to mid-May in the lunar calendar, mainly using nets. The autumn season is from late June to early September in the lunar calendar, mainly using trawls. As for the harvesting of shellfish, it can be collected along the coast at any time. The Nvgv (Nvgu) and Shuangbu areas within the Qingdao area bay are particularly abundant, with harvests even in winter.

Japanese Fishing

The Japanese began fishing in this city around 1914, following the Japanese army. Due to the various advantages given by their government, the most prosperous period was around 1916, when they almost seized our fishing grounds and occupied them. In 1915 and 1916, Qingdao had over 130 Japanese fishing boats. Currently, there are still 45 boats. The production of "Jiaji fish" (加級魚) along the Qingdao coast (this fish is a high-quality food, worth about five or six cents per pound) is extremely abundant and occupies an important sales market in this city. This kind of fresh fish is sold throughout the year, mostly caught by the Japanese. During the spring and autumn fishing seasons, the Japanese use large sailing ships or steamers to fish in the Haizhou area, while smaller boats travel to Shuilingshan Island, Daxiaogong Island, Talian Island, and the 千里島 (Thousand Mile Island) area. Even in winter when there are fewer fish, they send small boats to the south of Talian Island to harvest. A large sailing ship can earn over 7,000 yuan per year, while a small boat can earn over 2,000 yuan. The catch of our Chinese fishing boats is far less than that. Also, around 1916, the Japanese government, to encourage the catching of croaker, specially selected five sailing ships with excellent performance and provided funds, ordering them to go to Talian Island and Shidao in Laoshan Bay to try to catch croaker. Each ship averaged about 500 yuan in catch. Since then, the Japanese have often caught croaker in these places in winter. The fishing tools used by the Japanese include line fishing, cast nets, lift nets, drift nets, trawls, and diving equipment. Besides the Jiaji fish, which is the most numerous, there are also sharks, flounder, sea perch, pomfret, abalone, sea cucumber, and agar.

Protecting Fisheries

The coastal areas of Qi are originally rich fishing areas in our country, and the coastal areas of Qingdao have particularly large yields. However, because our Chinese fishermen adhere to old methods and do not seek new knowledge, this great maritime profit is seized by foreigners. In 1914, when the Japanese army occupied Qingdao, Japanese fishermen came along and encroached and harvested without being restrained. It was not until 1927, when the Bohai Fleet came to Qingdao to garrison, that measures were taken to protect fisheries, maintain maritime rights, and divide the area between the Yellow Sea and Bohai Sea into four zones: the first zone from south of Cangzhou Island to the vicinity of Haizhou; the second zone from north of Cangzhou Island to the Chengshantou area; the third zone from Chengshantou to the border between Huang County and Zhaoyuan; and the fourth zone from the border between Huang and Zhao counties to the nearby sea north of the Dagu River. Warships were dispatched to each zone to protect them. During the fishing season, in addition to protecting fisheries and maintaining order, they also cracked down on steamships forcibly buying fish and foreign fishing boats entering territorial waters to fish. They were able to effectively intervene, and the practice of Japanese crossing the sea to fish was reduced somewhat. Recently, the Hebei-Shandong Marine Fisheries Administration established an office in Qingdao and rented two steamships to engage in protection. In the future, our country's fisheries should gradually develop. (September 6)

News from Wutun and Wuzha Roads

Wutun Road Expected to be Completed Soon, Wuzha Road Under Active Construction

Wuhu correspondence: The Wuhu-Tunxi Road is one of the largest construction projects of this year by the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction. The Huihang Road has already been opened to traffic. Once the Wutun Road is completed, it can be connected to that road. With convenient transportation between Wuhu and Hangzhou, the products of southern Anhui will flow unimpeded, which is of great importance to culture and commerce. Recently, Liu Yiyan, the Director of the Department of Construction, has appointed Jin Youzhu, a technical officer, as the supervising committee member for the road. The road starts from Wuhu, crosses Xuancheng to Ningguo, passes through Jixi, and reaches Tunxi. The most difficult section, Ningguo to Jixi, is nearing completion. It is expected that by the end of this year, Wuhu can be connected to Jixi. In the past, it took people from various counties in Huizhou seven or eight days to travel to Wuhu. In the future, it will only take one day.

After the Jiangnan Railway Company held a groundbreaking ceremony for the construction of the Wuzha Railway, Hong Shen, the chief engineer, was responsible for actively carrying it out in Wuhu. No less than four or five thousand workers are working day and night on earth filling. The Wuhu to Wangzhi section is expected to be completed this year, and the Wangzhi to Sunjiabu section will also be completed next spring. After that section is completed, the Wusun section will be opened to traffic first. Currently, long-distance telephones are being installed and are expected to be operational within three months. More than eighty culverts and the Ningxiang Great Iron Bridge are all out for tender. (5th)

Songjiang County Asks for Funds to Repair Seawalls

The Jinshanzui seawall in this county was in danger last year. Xu Baikui, Director of the Construction Bureau, repaired it, converting the second and third sections into reinforced concrete structures. A Shanghai construction company contracted the work, which cost a considerable amount. However, the reinforced concrete structure could not withstand the impact of the waves and was not as durable as the old method of wooden stakes and stone embankments. It gradually collapsed, and the effect was minimal. The other day, a hurricane struck, and the people of Songjiang were very worried. Fortunately, there was no danger. However, if the seawall is not repaired for a long time, it is feared that danger will occur when the autumn flood arrives. The lives and property of the people of Songjiang are greatly affected. Last month, Gao Yihan, a supervising commissioner of the Supervisory Yuan, inspected the seawall and believed that the Jinshanzui seawall needed to be repaired. He requested the provincial government to allocate funds for repairs on behalf of the people. Now, Jin Zhuan of the county government, based on the dangerous condition of the seawall, has submitted a report to the provincial government requesting the allocation of funds for seawall repairs and has also submitted a valuation report.

Suzhou's Dean Lin Goes to Shanghai for Inspection

Lin Biao, the President of the Jiangsu High Court, went to Shanghai by car yesterday (the 6th) to inspect the new buildings of the Caohejing Second Prison, which are about to be completed, and also to inspect the Shanghai Special District Local Court and the detention center.

Completion of Tianping Road Project

Tianping Mountain in Mudu Township is the most famous scenic spot in Wu County. However, transportation is inconvenient, and tourists have to walk there. Now, the Second District Office has initiated the construction of Tianping Road (from Mudu directly to the foot of Tianping Mountain), which has been completed. A traffic ceremony will be held on the 10th of this month. The Department of Construction and the county government have been requested to send personnel to participate. After this, vehicles can go directly from Suzhou to Tianping Mountain.

Wuxi Rice Boat Robbed in Wangting

Wuxi Wanlongcheng Rice Store hired a boat to transport more than one hundred shi of brown rice to a rice store in Loumen, Suzhou, for delivery. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 6th) at 10:00 AM, when sailing near Wangting Township, they suddenly encountered a bandit boat with six or seven bandits armed with weapons. They robbed the boat, taking away more than one hundred yuan in cash and the boat owner Zhou Chunshan's clothes, etc., with a loss of about three hundred yuan.

The Enthusiastic Triumph of the Wuxi National Games

The Second District National Games were held in Wujin this time. The male and female athletes from this county, because of their skilled training and excellent results, caused the counties of Wujin, Yixing, and Jiangyin to be defeated. As a result, Wuxi won a total of seven general championships and classified championships. The remaining gold, silver, and bronze medals, silk flags, and mirror frames were countless, accounting for two-thirds of the conference. Yesterday, the male and female athletes returned in full dress. When the train passed through Loshe and Shitangwan in the county, the villagers set off firecrackers to celebrate, and the shouts of joy mingled together. When they arrived at the Wuxi station, the station was crowded with people, flags were flying, and firecrackers and military music were played together. All the athletes were happy and excited. The enthusiastic situation was no less than when the revolutionary army arrived in Wuxi during the Northern Expedition. After the athletes got off the train, they marched around the city in formation to the park. Zang Fogen, the Director of the Education Bureau, prepared refreshments to reward the three armies and held a consolation meeting. Director Zang and Pu Yicheng, the representative of the county party headquarters, gave speeches, which were very grand for a time.

The Second Day of the Autumn Cocoon Market Opening

Yesterday was the second day of the autumn cocoon market opening. Goods from the southwest countryside were still pouring in, and the cocoons were also of good quality. The Zhongqiao Dachang Cocoon Firm received seventy or eighty dan of goods, with a high price of forty yuan. Next was the Hutai Yongtaihe, which received about seventy dan of goods, with a high price of thirty-five yuan and inferior goods at twenty-five yuan. Other cocoon firms in Zhangcun, Sitou, Yanqiao, Hujiadu, Chang'anqiao, Dongting, Bashiqiao, Zhangjingqiao, Zhouxin Township, Nanqiao, Shitangwan, Shitang Township, Daqiangmen, Qianzhou, Loshe, Zhiqi, Beiqifang, and Meicun also received a large influx of goods, with prices hovering around thirty yuan. The Qianqiao Yangting and Zhangshe areas are scheduled to open tomorrow. Yesterday, the Cocoon Industry Association received thirty-four more applications to open, bringing the total to one hundred and eleven. In Meicun Township in the tenth district, the Tailun and Juyuan firms arbitrarily reduced cocoon prices when they saw that there were many cocoon sellers, which aroused dissatisfaction among the villagers, who made trouble with the two firms. Later, the town's security regiment came out to maintain order and ordered them to follow the association's resolution and handle the matter with discretion before it could be quelled. Also, yesterday, more than ten villagers from the northern road border between Wuxi and Cheng in Taipingqiao Gongyichang Cocoon Firm in the sixth district brought cocoons to sell. The firm immediately lowered the price because the cocoons were soft. At that time, a few hooligans intentionally made trouble, making a lot of noise outside the firm, which was unreasonable. Ji Quansheng, the manager of the firm, came out to persuade them, but somehow fell to the ground and died. The cocoon-selling villagers, seeing that a disaster had occurred, all scattered.

Jiangyin Provincial Department Investigates Old Tax Debts

The Department of Finance stated that the total amount of provincial taxes owed by various counties in this province from 1927 to 1931 reached more than seven million (excluding various surtaxes). It has already formulated measures to clear old taxes and appointed Li Guoqi as the Jiangyin Tax Clearing Commissioner, who came to Cheng on the 4th. After contacting the county government, it was found that Jiangyin owed about two million one hundred thousand yuan in old land taxes from 1927 to 1931, of which nearly nine hundred thousand yuan was owed to the provincial treasury. The proposed method of clearing and urging payment this time is to divide the county into seven districts, with one commissioner assigned to each district to copy the amounts owed by the handling clerks and guarantors from the land tax office and go to various townships to check and verify them. These measures will be implemented after Commissioner Li returns to the province and obtains approval.

Drugs Seized on Zhengda Steamer

He Yalin, the Director of the Fourth Branch of the Cheng Drug Investigation Office, received a report from Xu Asan of Shanghai that the Datong Company's Shanghai-Yangzhou Zhengda steamer was carrying a large amount of morphine, red pills, etc. After receiving the report, Director He waited for the steamer to arrive at Huangtiangang from Shanghai at about 10:00 PM on the 4th, then took the Fuyan patrol boat to the steamer's laogui (engineer) room and found several pounds of morphine, worth four or five hundred yuan, more than ten pounds of red pills, about one or two hundred thousand pills, and a full set of smoking paraphernalia. He then detained the laogui (yesterday's telegram mistakenly said mate), Tang Xinglan, a native of Yangjing Town, Pudong, and the cook, a native of Liuhe. The Zhengda steamer, because it had no laogui, immediately dropped anchor. At that time, the Jiangyin Datong branch, for the sake of passengers and goods, urgently needed to go to Yangzhou and repeatedly requested Director He to have Zhang Xinglan temporarily bailed out by the staff Wang Ying. The steamer sailed to Yangzhou at about 1:00 AM this morning (the 5th) and will hand over Zhang to the Zhen for interrogation after finding another steamer's laogui.

The Descendant of a Zhenjiang Warlord Drifts to Zhenjiang

The late warlord Zhang Zongchang had twenty-three concubines during his lifetime. After he was assassinated by Zheng Zhishi, his family gave the concubines money to dismiss them. His thirteenth concubine, Wu Ruiji, is now twenty-four years old and a native of Fengtian. She is of ordinary appearance. After getting money in Ping, she went to live in Shanghai. She became acquainted with a man surnamed Mou from Shangdang Township in this city and came to Zhenjiang to live for half a year. Wu was not accustomed to living in the countryside and broke up with Mou. Through Wang's introduction, she married Zhao Zhenhua, the former Director of the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau, and lived with him in the Anle Inn opened by Zhao on Nanmen Street, which was very harmonious. Last night, for some reason, they suddenly quarreled and then used force. They wrestled in a ball on Shengfu Road. After investigation, the police brought them to the Second Branch Bureau. Wu insisted on divorcing her husband. After Zhao inquired, he persuaded both parties to settle it peacefully outside.

The Neihe Dada Steamer Company's newly built small steamer (Gongxin) will be dedicated to the Zhenshao route and was launched on the 5th. It departs from Zhen every morning at 7:00 AM, arrives in Yangzhou at 9:00 AM to unload passengers, and then opens to Shao. It departs from Shao at 12:00 PM to Yangzhou and then departs from Yangzhou to Zhen at 2:00 PM. It has also negotiated terms with Fu Yun, Xiehe, and other eight companies, and will take turns to open to Qingjiang and other places on schedule, with uniform fares, to maintain business and benefit travelers.

Truth About the Jiashen Taozhuang Huge Theft Case

The Jiashen Taozhuang Town Taiheyuan Rice Store robbery case, which caused a great uproar, is still unknown. It is now known that Taiheyuan was exclusively opened by Sun Yancai, Chairman of the Jiashen Chamber of Commerce, and has been in business for decades. Its business is the largest in the county, and it has long been coveted by bandits. This time, the store had a sum of township funds, totaling more than 4,000 yuan, hidden in a silver box. Few outsiders knew about it, but the bandits knew about it. Taking advantage of the absence of manager Lu Chunling, they went together. When the partners were taking the money, the fellows were aware of it and intended to announce it. They were threatened by the thieves with a pistol and allowed them to take away all the money. Therefore, a bullet was left behind when they left. It is a misunderstanding that the outside world says the thieves had their own keys. The water and land police and the local defense regiments have been notified to strictly search and arrest the bandits.

Hangzhou Security Office Executes Two Kidnappers

The Zhejiang Provincial Security Office, according to the Hang County and 临安 (Linan) County Governments, presented and escorted three bandit Yang Shouyu, Li Azhong, Han Youcai etc., involved in the kidnapping case of Yang Shizhen, son of Yang Zhiliang of Shuangtiaoba. After interrogation, it was found that the bandit Yang Shouyu lived next to Yang Zhiliang and knew that he had money. He had the idea of kidnapping and redeeming him, and invited Li Azhong, Han Youcai, and the executed La Jinmao and the fugitive Big Foot A Lian and others. On the night of the 23rd day of the third month of the old calendar this year, they went to his house and kidnapped his four-year-old son and hid him in La Jinmao's house. They got a ransom of 230 yuan and returned the hostage. Except for Han Youcai, whose circumstances were lighter and was sentenced to imprisonment, the rest were sentenced to death according to the law. Yesterday (the 6th) at 8:00 AM, staff were sent to bring Yang Shouyu and Li Azhong to verify their identities and tie them to the execution ground outside Qingbomen to be executed by shooting.

Local News

Sun Tonggang, in a Great National Flight, Flew From Beijing to Shanghai Yesterday

Participated in the Naming Ceremony of the Five Aircrafts, Will Fly to Hangzhou on the 10th, and Return to Germany for Research After One Month. The Municipal Government Hosted a Banquet Last Night and the Party Headquarters Hosted a Lunch Today.

Sun Tonggang, a young pilot studying in Germany, previously flew a single-wing land plane from Germany to his motherland over a long distance, experiencing all kinds of hardships and earning a national reputation. He then returned to his ancestral home in Shandong Province to visit his relatives. Later, due to the enthusiastic welcome letters and telegrams from people all over the country, Sun decided to make a national flight with the aim of saving the country through aviation. On the 5th, he flew from Jinan with Wang Zuwen, passing through Xuzhou and Bengbu, and arrived in Beijing. After a short stay, he flew to Shanghai from Beijing at 9:45 yesterday morning and arrived safely at Hongqiao Airport at 11:50. Various agencies and groups in this city sent representatives to the airport to welcome him. The enthusiastic situation was extremely grand. The municipal government hosted a banquet for Sun last night at 7:00 PM. This afternoon, the city party headquarters hosted a lunch at the Shanghai United Association. Sun said that after participating in the naming ceremony of the five aircrafts in Shanghai, he will fly to Hangzhou on the morning of the 10th and then fly to various places. It is expected that the entire trip can be completed in about a month, and then he will go to Germany to continue his research. The details are recorded as follows:

Welcoming Personnel

The various sectors of this city who went to Hongqiao Airport to welcome him yesterday included Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, representing Mayor Wu, Zhang Xiang, Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Command, Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Education Bureau, Li Dachao, Section Chief of the Municipal Government, Wang Zhicheng, representing the Security Office, Zhang Xingbai of the City Party Headquarters, Lin Wojiang, Secretary-General of the Chinese Aviation Association, He Zhuoxian, Director of the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, Chen Wenlin, Director of the Xiamen Aviation Office of the Navy Department, Pan Dingxin, Chief of the Mechanical Section, Zeng Yijing, Director of the Aircraft Manufacturing Office of the Navy, Huang Baoxian, Manager of China National Aviation Corporation, Wu Shan of the Chinese Road Association, Huang Zao Xiong of the City Education Association, Zheng Chengqing of the City Chamber of Commerce, Shao Xubai of the General Labour Union, Lu Jingtu of the National Postal Workers Union, Jarlot, Chairman of the Western Aviation Association, as well as the Seamen's Union and the Qingnian Flying Home Sun Tonggang Jun (He Zhuoxian Photography)

Representatives from various agencies and groups, such as the Two Special Party Headquarters, the South Goods Industry Union, the Shipping Guild, the Tea Making Guild, the First District Water and Electricity Union, the Tenth District Cotton Spinning Guild, and the Wharf Industry Union, totaled about 300 people.

Careful Security

Those on duty at the airport yesterday included one squad of the First and Middle Team of the Public Security Bureau and more than forty police officers from the Sixth District First Branch, who were stationed at the airport to keep watch, strictly protecting and prohibiting idlers from entering. The Aviation Administration also sent more than ten soldiers to guard and patrol the area. The airport police also helped maintain order and protection. A temporary shed was erected in the field for the welcoming personnel to rest, with a white cloth banner hanging above that read "Chinese Aviation Association Welcomes Aviator Sun Tonggang." A cross mark was also formed with white cloth in the center of the field to make it easier for Sun to identify and land.

Landing Situation

The representatives of various groups who went to welcome him held up white cloth banners with the words "Welcome Chinese Youth Pilot" written on them. The same welcome slogans were also written on white cloth banners behind the cars. All the welcoming personnel were excited and enthusiastic. From about 9:00 AM they waited until 11:50 AM, when the plane driven by Sun arrived in the sky above the airport. The whole scene erupted in thunderous applause that resounded through the clouds. The plane circled in the sky for several weeks, making a brief performance before the fuselage gradually descended. Sun frequently waved his hand to indicate his intentions. After the plane stopped, Secretary-General Yu, Lin Wojiang, Zhang Xiang and others approached the front of the plane to welcome him, shaking hands one by one. Li Dachao, a section chief of the municipal government, also presented a bouquet of flowers on behalf of the citizens of Shanghai, along with close relatives Liu Zhongping and Zheng Jisheng, as well as two young ladies. Sun accepted with a smile and expressed his gratitude. The Tianchu MSG factory then presented Sun with gas masks and two small suitcases of MSG, with the words "Self-Defense for the Country" and "Work Hard for Extra Meals" written on them. At that time, Wang Zuwen immediately distributed the printed materials brought from Jinan to the welcoming personnel. Then, accompanied by Lin Wojiang, Sun and Wang took a car to the Aviation Association for rest. The municipal government also designated Cangzhou Hotel on Jingansi Road as their accommodation. Sun is now twenty-six years old and is wearing a yellow cloth Zhongshan suit with a gray wool vest and yellow twill shorts, wearing yellow leather shoes. He has a burly body and full of energy. Having been washed by the sun for a long time, his skin is red-purple. At a glance, he is known to be a determined and brave aviation hero. Wang Zuwen is Sun's classmate and is about the same age as Sun, as well as being burly and strong.

A Glimpse of the Fuselage

The aircraft driven by Sun is a German 克伦姆 (Klem) single-wing aircraft with five cylinders, weighing 465 pounds, with a load capacity of 235 pounds, 90 horsepower, a normal speed of 145 kilometers per hour, and a top speed of 170 kilometers per hour. The wings are yellow in color, made of wood, and the fuselage is painted with the party emblem. On both sides of the fuselage are written the words "Save the Country Through Aviation".各界歡迎孫君留影 (徐天章攝)A group photo of all circles welcoming Sun Jun (Xu Tianzhang Photography)

This aircraft was purchased by Sun at his own expense a year and a half ago. The price of the aircraft was 18,000 marks, which is about 20,000 yuan in Chinese currency. The fuselage is slightly larger than the aircraft driven by Chen Wenlin, the current director of the Naval Aviation Office, four years ago.

Remarks

After Sun and Wang got off the plane, they shook hands with the welcoming personnel one by one. They then made remarks to the reporter group, saying that they departed from Nanjing at 9:45 this morning (i.e., yesterday morning) and planned to arrive here at 11:00. Later, due to headwinds on the way and because they circled over Suzhou for several weeks, their arrival was slightly delayed. They decided to participate in the naming ceremony of the five aircrafts on the 9th of this month and will fly to Hangzhou on the 10th. They plan to stay in Hangzhou for a week and then continue flying to Anqing, Hankou, Changsha, Zhumadian, Zhengzhou, and Luoyang. At that time, depending on the amount of oil, they will decide whether to fly to Lanzhou, then return to Kaifeng, and then go to Baoding, Datong, Zhangjiakou, and Suiyuan Beiping to visit the war zone. Then they will fly through Tianjin to Qingdao and back to Jinan to complete the national flight. As for Guangzhou and Hong Kong, they do not plan to go there again because they have already been there on their last return to China. They also do not plan to go to Yunnan and Sichuan because there is no oil station equipment. Their original plan for this flight was to travel with Feng Yong, but Feng's purpose was slightly different, so they gave up. After the national flight is completed, they will schedule a trip to Germany to continue their research. The purpose of this flight, at the request of all sectors of society, is to awaken the Chinese people to save the country through aviation.

Distributing Flyers

When Sun departed from Jinan this time, he distributed flyers along the way to awaken compatriots across the country to practice aviation to save the country. The flyer says that China is accumulating days and the foreign insults are invading, the mountains and rivers are broken, and the survival of the nation is at the last moment of life and death. In this world of air force competition, there is no way to save the country without promoting aviation. Therefore, they are making a national flight to awaken the attention and awareness of aviation among the people of the country, unite the strength of the entire country from top to bottom, and actively promote aviation, learn to drive and manufacture, cultivate talents, complete national defense, and resist foreign insults. Further, they will organize a strong air force to recover lost land, eradicate national shame, and break the insult of the sick man of East Asia, so that the country can reach the first rank in the world and restore the brilliant history of the four thousand-year-old civilized country of China. In short, it is to awaken compatriots across the country to save the country and revive the nation through aviation.龚叔窜摄Gong Shucuan photographed the municipal government's banquet for Sun Jun.

Sun's Brief Biography

Sun's brief biography is as follows: Mr. Sun is currently twenty-six years old, from Jiaohe, Hebei Province, and is the younger brother of Sun Jixuan, the commander of the 20th Division. He graduated from the Fifth Middle School of Hebei Province and then served in Han Fuju's army for two years. In the twelfth year of the Republic (1923), he was sent by the National Government to study in Germany. He entered the National Haberkson School and the Siemens factory in Germany for a one-year internship. Subsequently, he entered the flight instructor school and studied technical flying under the German technician Fissler. He also spent half a year in the glider department of the German Aviation School. Finally, he graduated from the National Chiao Tung University Aviation School this summer. He plans to study aircraft manufacturing in Germany after completing a long-distance flight across Eurasia and a nationwide circumnavigation.

City Government's Banquet

Yesterday at 7 PM, Yu Hongjun, the secretary-general of the municipal government, representing Mayor Wu Tiecheng, hosted a banquet at the municipal government reception office on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession to welcome Mr. Sun and Mr. Wang. Celebrities from all walks of life were also invited to attend, including Sun Tonggang, Wang Zuwen, Zhu Ziqiao, Yu Qiaqing, President Zheng Hongnian of Jinan University, Acting Garrison Commander Zhang Xiang, Secretary-General Lin Wojang of the Aviation Association, Superintendent Si Haian of the Jianghai Customs, directors of various bureaus of the municipal government Wen Hongen, Pan Gongzhan, Shen Yi, Xu Peihuang, Cai Zengji, Wu Xingya, Jin Liren, Li Tingan, Bai from the municipal party headquarters, Qian Xinzhi and Lin Kanghou from the banking sector, Speaker Shi Liangcai of the Municipal Council, Chairman Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Tang Shixuan, section chief Li Dachao, and others from the municipal government, totaling more than thirty people. During the banquet, Secretary-General Yu delivered a welcome speech on behalf of Mayor Wu, stating that Mr. Sun's return from Germany had brought honor to the country, and his courageous act of flying across the country to promote aviation for national salvation was truly admirable to the entire nation. He mentioned that when Colonel Lindbergh came to China, our country also hoped to have someone like Colonel Lindbergh. He praised Mr. Sun's courageous act as the first in China's aviation industry and as China's Lindbergh. Finally, Mr. Yu praised Mr. Sun for his insightful vision of aviation for national salvation and his efforts to promote and inspire the interest and aspirations of young people across the country in aviation, encouraging them to join the aviation industry, thereby cultivating more aviation talents for the country's use. He noted that in today's nationwide call for aviation for national salvation, there is a concern about having airplanes but lacking talent, and Mr. Sun's contribution is invaluable. Mr. Sun then delivered a thank-you speech. The guests and hosts parted happily at around 9 PM.

Today's and Tomorrow's Banquets

Upon hearing the news of Mr. Sun's arrival in Shanghai, all sectors of the city plan to hold banquets to welcome him. After consultation with the Aviation Association, the schedule is arranged as follows: At noon on the 7th, the Municipal Party Headquarters will host a banquet at the Shanghai United Entertainment Club in the Silk Industry Building. At 7 PM, Chen Wenlin, director of the Naval Xiamen Aviation Office, and Zeng Yijing, director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office, will host a banquet at the Naval United Entertainment Club. On the morning of the 8th, Mr. Sun will fly to the Songhu area to view the January 28th battle zone and circumnavigate the entire city. At that time, Lin Wojang of the Aviation Association may accompany him. He will rest in his residence in the afternoon. On the afternoon of the 9th, he will attend the naming ceremony of the five aircraft of the Aviation Association and will perform an aerial display. Captain Foulos, the leader of the British Aviation Association, also plans to host a banquet, and the date is currently being arranged. Mr. Sun and Mr. Wang visited the Aviation Association yesterday and automatically joined the association as members.

The Joint Relief Association for the Yellow River Flood Discusses Relief Methods

It is resolved to allocate 50,000 yuan for urgent relief in four major cases.

The Shanghai Charitable Organizations Raising Relief Funds for the Yellow River Flood Joint Relief Association held its first executive committee joint meeting at Renji Hall on Yunnan Road at 4 PM yesterday to discuss relief methods. The details are recorded as follows:

Attendees

Attendees included Wang Xiaolai, Zhu Ziqiao, Zheng Hongnian, Wen Lanting, Weng Yinchu, Pan Xulun, Wang Peiyuan, Guan Yunnong, Qian Jinping, Chen Liangyu, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng (all representing), Li Zizai, Chen Aishi, Gu Xinyi, Shao Ruxin, Master Mingdao, Wang Junsheng, Hu Fengxiang, Huang Bodu, Huang Hanzhi, Zheng Zhongshan, Zhou Weishi, Gu Jisheng, Guan Jiongzhi, Guang Yunsheng, and more than thirty others. Chairman's Report

Discussion Items

(1) The disaster situation in the provinces along the Yellow River is severe, and relief is urgently needed. How should the 50,000 yuan of relief funds raised by the association be allocated and distributed quickly for urgent relief in the affected areas? It was resolved to allocate 30,000 yuan (silver dollars) to Shandong, to be distributed by the Jisheng Association, and 20,000 yuan (silver dollars) to Henan, to be distributed by the Red Cross Society and the Chinese Buddhist Association.

(2) How should the association's relief funds be raised? It was resolved to ask the three directors of the fundraising team to establish and proceed immediately, and to send personnel to the association to handle the matter.

(3) Please ask the directors of each group to start organizing and proceeding immediately, and please come to the meeting in person or appoint a representative daily to handle the affairs of this group. It was resolved to send letters to the directors of each section, asking them to consider the urgency of the disaster, start organizing and dispatching personnel for regular office work immediately, and come to the meeting daily in person or appoint a representative to handle affairs every day.

(4) It was stipulated that a regular meeting should be held every Wednesday. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

Workers at the Jiangnan Rubber Factory in Jiangnan Announced a Strike Yesterday Morning

Opposing the factory's reduction of wages and proposing seven demands

The Jiangnan Rubber Factory on Wuhua Road, Hongkou, Shanghai, recently announced on the 3rd of this month that it would reduce the wages of female workers in the sneaker department by one-third due to declining business (the original wage was 6 cents per pair, now reduced to 4 cents). The female workers expressed their opposition and reported to the Fourth District Rubber Workers Union for assistance. After receiving the report, the union sent Song Yexian and Zhang Xunzhai to negotiate with the factory. Zhou Yiyan, the manager of the factory, received them and replied that if they did not agree to the wage reduction, he would dismiss all 50-odd female workers in the department and recruit new workers instead, resulting in a fruitless negotiation. The union prepared a document to petition the Party and government organs and the General Labor Union for mediation. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 4th, the factory forced the female workers in the department to sign a document acknowledging the wage reduction. Upon hearing the news, the workers throughout the factory were outraged and unanimously went on strike yesterday morning, raising seven demands: (1) Wages should be paid as usual during the strike. (2) Members should not be dismissed without reason; the union must be notified before a member is dismissed. (3) Wages should not be reduced. (4) Workers should not be oppressed without reason. (5) The factory must distribute work evenly. (6) Membership in the union should not be a condition for employment. (7) Yu Kunru, the factory's lackey who reduces wages and undermines the labor movement, should be expelled from the factory. The strike will not end until these demands are met. The union has reported the strike situation to the Party and government organs yesterday and requested immediate mediation.

Party and Government Organs Mediated the Jardine Matheson Company Dispute Yesterday

It was decided to meet again this morning to discuss solutions.

After the British-owned Jardine Matheson Tugboat Company dismissed a large number of Chinese workers, all the Chinese workers rose up in opposition and petitioned the Party and government organs for mediation to maintain their livelihood. At 1 PM yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau sent mediator Zhu Guilin, and the Municipal Party Headquarters sent cadre Ku Weixiong to jointly seek solutions. The company stated that the reason for dismissing 44 dockworkers in various locations was due to sluggish business, and they agreed to pay each worker half a month's wage as severance pay. As for the ten boats, including Nos. 24, and 47 workers, it was a job transfer. After negotiations by the Party and government organs, it was decided to meet again this morning to discuss solutions.

The Ministry of Finance Established a Loan of 12 Million Yuan from Shanghai Banks

Secured by customs duties and underwritten by eight banks including the Central Bank, it is specifically used for urgent relief for the Yellow River flood.

The Ministry of Finance and eight banks including the Shanghai Central Bank and the Bank of China negotiated to establish a new loan totaling 12 million yuan to deal with urgent relief for the Yellow River flood. It is secured by customs duties. The New Voice News Agency has learned the details as follows:

Total Loan Amount

After returning to China at the end of last month, Finance Minister Song Ziwen, in view of the severity of the Yellow River flood, with breaches in Shandong and Henan provinces, and millions of victims in the affected areas in dire need of food, should immediately allocate funds for relief. While in Shanghai, he negotiated with the banking sector in Shanghai to borrow money to deal with urgent relief for the Yellow River flood, the total amount of which is 12 million yuan.

Eight Banks Underwrite

The underwriting banks for the Yellow River flood urgent relief loan are the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, China South Bank, Yanye Bank, Jincheng Bank, Dalu Bank, and Siming Bank. The underwriting methods are divided into three types: 2 million yuan, 1 million yuan, and 500,000 yuan, which are underwritten by the eight banks separately.

Customs Duty Guarantee

The collateral for this new loan is monthly appropriation of funds from the customs duty revenue to be repaid within one year. Minister Song has already reached an agreement with the banking sector in Shanghai yesterday, and a formal contract will be signed in Shanghai. The rumor of 15 million yuan is actually a mistake for 12 million yuan.
