Shen Bao National Products Weekly

National Products Forum

The Fate of Chinese National Products

— Yang An

The recent promotion of national products in China can be described as shouting at the top of one's voice and doing everything possible. Since January 28th, we have been talking about boycotting Japanese goods and using national products every day. The numbers recorded in newspapers, the speeches delivered in meetings, and the propaganda on the streets, I ask, how much have we actually boycotted Japanese goods? How much have we actually used national products? Do Chinese people have accurate investigations? Detailed statistics? If we examine it, we don't know whether we will be covered in sweat and feel ashamed to the point of having nowhere to go? The results of one year have neither harmed the Japanese in the slightest, but have instead fueled their rampant behavior. The Japanese once said that the amount of goods they received from the boycott in the Chinese market last year was twice the amount they sold in Southeast Asia and India. Why should they have any worries? Although their words may be exaggerated, the facts are like this, how can we remain silent? A friend who returned from Japan said that although the Japanese promotion of national products does not have the name of national control, it already has the reality of industry control. The strategies they adopt are six:

㈠ Production Restriction: For a certain factory, based on its needs, if it is assumed that there must be ten, then more than ten are not allowed to be established, so as not to oversupply and cause price competition, which would prevent it from standing in a stable position.

㈡ Division of Labor: For a certain industry, in addition to the same kind of manufacturing, those with related relationships, such as iron smelting, steel refining, and installation, adopt a division of labor and cooperation method to seek economy.

㈢ Joint Purchase of Raw Materials: The joint agency purchases raw materials from the same place, is responsible for transportation, and the price is low and the transportation is fast.

㈣ Research to Reduce Costs: Each factory recruits talents and pays attention to the improvement of products and the reduction of costs.

㈤ Pay Attention to Export Combinations: There are more than 140 Japanese export combinations around the world, proceeding step by step, leaving no loophole. There are more than 40 export combinations to China. The government tries its best to encourage them. Last year, the subsidy for the import combination in the Far East was 1.8 million yuan. There are three established methods: no unnecessary competition is allowed, no arbitrary price increases or decreases are allowed, and no infringement of business position is allowed. The expenditure on investigation fees is never stingy, and the travel expenses of people sent by various industries are also subsidized by the government, which shows its intention.

㈥ Pay Attention to Sales Combinations: The industry association has great power. The government and the industry association are currently paying attention to the activities of sales merchants. Recently, they have been promoting Dutch, Javanese, Indian, and Singaporean merchants to sell for them, using extremely low prices and extremely generous benefits to induce them in many ways, which has achieved great results.

In Japan, national products are almost used everywhere, but the government still sets up a national product promotion committee, stipulates a national product memorial day, and the intention to promote national products is everywhere in newspapers, magazines, meetings, and roads. Recently, the government convened ministers, experts from various industries to study the non-national products currently used in Japan, and there are more than 140 kinds. After various studies, more than 120 kinds can be replaced by national products, and only 20 kinds have to use foreign goods temporarily, which shows their attention. Recently, Mr. Zhang Gongquan went to Japan for sightseeing. What he saw and heard was mostly like this. People are advancing while we are retreating. People are knives and chopping boards, we are fish and meat. People have sharpened their swords and are waiting, but we are indifferent and unmoved. The fate of Chinese national products is like this, what could be more painful. It is also said that if the government agencies in Japan purchase goods and the purchasers are careless and misuse foreign goods, they will not be reimbursed to show punishment. The spirit of unity between officials and the people is like this, can the people of our country remain unmoved?

National Products Talk

The Life and Death of National Product Factories

— Tian Ran

An industrialist with a lot of experience said: During the National Products Year, everyone said good things. In my opinion, the future of national products has reached the point of no remedy. If there is no improvement, I am afraid that they will all close down in five years. When he said this kind of discouraging words, I asked him for the truth. He said that the facts are like this, and there is no denying it. If you compare the national product factories in China with others, the first is that the capital is not as good as others, the second is that the knowledge is not as good as others, the third is that the experience is not as good as others, the fourth is that the unity of doing things is not as good as others, the fifth is that the cost is not as cheap as others, and the sixth is that the products are not as good as others. It is already extremely dangerous and extremely pitiful. In addition, all countries in the world are currently feeling overproduction. One's products can't be sold to another country, and another's products are desperately trying to be sold to countries with immature industries. Everyone wants to find a way out. After looking around, only China can still turn around. They are the residences for their products. If you are like this, and he is like this, the result is that they all build deep trenches and high fortresses and use tariffs as the only weapon, and they use China as the only market for all countries in the world to sell their national products. How can it be possible for the Chinese people to have some means to fight against them? How can it be possible for the Chinese people to have some preparations to deal with them? As a result, is there still room for the existence of Chinese goods factories?

National Products in the Eyes of Women

— Zhang Mengzhao

The biggest customers of goods on the market are of course women in general. The wheel of the times in 1932 has not yet passed, and they are already looking for and buying new products in 1933. These women who are the prelude to the times are all knowledgeable, leisurely classes, modern female students, aristocratic ladies, etc. They neither have a correct understanding of national products, nor do national products have standards for them to use as goals. Therefore, they unconsciously and naturally serve as obligatory salespersons for foreign goods of imperialists! This kind of atmosphere will spread to female workers working in factories and women in the interior, emulating the frenzy of women in big cities, how heartbreaking?

Promoting national products... has been going on for several years, and it is simply tiring to hear. Only now are we gradually progressing with the wheel of the times. National Products Week, National Products Year, National Products Commercial Ground, National Products Company, consumer cooperatives, everyone is working together, shouting and doing, but national products in the eyes of women are still like Liu Yi at sea. In the three famous companies, if we go to tour them separately, the liveliness and loneliness are obvious facts. The national products companies welcomed by women in general are few and far between. There are probably only a few famous national products stores that they are happy to visit. Now they are gradually paying attention to the Chinese National Products Company. It is unknown whether they can be persevering and always recognize clearly, or whether it is still a question!

The Three Eras of National Products

— Ke Ding'an

In the past, before the sea ban was lifted, everything that the Chinese people needed for their daily use was made from their own raw materials and by their own manufacture. This can be said to be a pure national product era, or the first era of national products.

After the sea ban was lifted, people in general felt that foreign goods were beautiful in style and convenient to use, so they changed their minds and unanimously purchased foreign goods. Later, some people carefully observed the foreign goods and felt that there was no great difficulty in their structure and imitation. So they went to their raw material suppliers and bought raw materials like returning onions, and then asked their technicians (referring to foreign technicians) to manufacture them in the same way. This can be said to be the national product imitation era, or the second era of national products.

Up to now, many Chinese people have clear minds. They deeply know that such imitation of others, purchasing of others' raw materials, and producing crudely and shoddily to supply to the Chinese people, you want to know how discerning the Chinese people are under such a trend, will he still come to use your warehouse of crudely and shoddily produced products? So their minds are relatively fresh, they want to study where the raw materials are produced? Does China have it after all? What kind of style should the products be to suit the general public? What kind of quality should the products be to be durable? How can the sales of the products be smooth and unimpeded? Study carefully and strive for excellence, even if his products cannot gain a foothold in the national product industry!

But now, there are still people who are like the second era of national products, and they are even afraid that the imitation is not enough, even the bottle of a cosmetic product, if the foreign product is a wine jar style, we are also a wine jar style, and the box for filling the bottle, if they are printed in yellow, we also print in yellow. This is simply too similar to imitate. Haven't you seen foreign merchants often sue Chinese merchants for imitation in the newspapers? When it comes to the result, either the imitated products are all confiscated, or they are ordered to stop business. Although this is the means of the imperialists, the Chinese's deliberate imitation is indeed true.

This is really a very sad sentence. Among national products, except for some products that have not been fully improved; nine out of ten can be said to be imitations of foreign products. So I have said long ago that national products should be thought of from the aspect of creation. The things that are manufactured should transcend everything. Not only should they surpass all domestic products, but they should also surpass foreign goods. That's how to cater to the psychology of modern Chinese people. If you insist on the old ways, failure will be in front of you.

Most of the people who operate national product businesses are merchants. Although there are also some with superior knowledge, there are also quite a few who only seek profit and disregard everything. Because of this, his products are perfunctory and will never have a day to develop. I think that in order for the products to sell well, we should put in effort in all aspects.

There are really too few people in China who study industrial arts and crafts. The government does not have a way to reward them, so many talents have been buried. If the people who operate national product businesses can unite with the people who study industrial arts and crafts and create many unique products, they will definitely shock the Chinese people!

In the current situation, it is really a mixed era of national products, or it can be said to be the third era of national products.

National Products Discussion

The "Boom Month" of National Products

— Xuan Wan

July and August (lunar calendar) is the time for various places to purchase goods, and it is also the time when our national product factories' goods sell well in the interior. There is a very common saying on the Shanghai market called "boom month". This probably refers to the second and third months of the spring and the current July and August丨Because the business in these months is booming, different from the usual months, but at this time, rural bankruptcy, the economic collapse in the interior, the extremely depressed taste, plus the Yellow River flood, the business in the Northwest is greatly affected, and the Zhuang customers in various places, although they always have to come out to purchase goods as usual and transport them back for sale in the second half of the year, however, as far as the impact is concerned, everything is not, and various bad phenomena also occur. Under the gift of this "boom month", the following findings have been made:

Regarding the customer's side: ㈠ Substandard goods are sold in abundance. This can prove that the purchasing power of the general public is extremely weak now. They give up the top-notch goods and don't add them, but only sell substandard goods on the active market. The decline of national products is the main reason.

The repayment is slow. According to the habit of merchants, tickets are usually issued every ten days, or cleared every month, but now they always delay. This also shows that the economy in the interior is tight and the turnover is not smooth, and the fundamental reason is naturally the slow sales.

Regarding their own aspects: ㈠ Price competition and internal strife among the industry is the most heartbreaking thing in our country's market. Now, because the market is not good, prices are falling, and they compete with each other and seek their own interests.

㈡ Manufacturing substandard goods to cater to customer psychology and specialize in making substandard goods to meet the market. In the minds of general merchants, they only want to make some profits from it, and they don't study the smooth production and sales of national products. Therefore, we have to take full responsibility for opening up this serious situation and actively proceed. The most heartbreaking internal strife and price competition make the Zhuang customers enjoy their profits, and the really buying public may not see the cheap price. This kind of inferior nature must first be eradicated from the root. The steps are: First, the industry associations should jointly determine the prices of goods, the selling prices should be the same, and they should be strictly observed. Second, notify the factories not to make substandard goods, and reduce the prices of the top-notch goods as much as possible to promote them and avoid confusion in the market. Then, they should gradually solve the fundamental problems such as how to enable national product factories to directly trade with buyers in the interior without going through merchants, and the cooperation between production and sales.

In the midst of wind and rain and the crisis is lurking everywhere, in this "boom month", how will the people in charge of national products consider the situation and exhaust their minds to save this already collapsed tide?

Promoting National Products and Mass Education

— Xing Guangyi

I have a kind of suspicion about education: that is, the higher the level of education, the more foreign goods are used. It seems that Chinese education is only teaching students to use foreign goods. This observation is proved by the fact that the level of education and the consumption of national products are in direct proportion. Then, to put it bluntly, why are we doing this kind of education?

Now the voice of promoting national products is rising, and everyone has discussed the promotion of national products a lot, but no one has paid attention to the relationship between national products and education itself, especially mass education.

It seems that the purpose of education is to become an official and seize money. As long as there is money, there is nothing that cannot be done. So they only seek to gain without working and despise production and manufacturing. Outside, there are even cheap, beautiful, charming and exquisite foreign goods that dazzle our eyes. So this impression is deeply engraved in the minds of the Chinese people, and they naturally increase their faith in foreign goods and are seduced by foreign goods. What ability does the popularization of education have to resist the tide? Some people say: "National products should be sold to the countryside丨" Of course, I also agree, but how can we sell national products to the countryside is a problem, and it can never be done out of thin air. Here, we should pay the most attention to mass education!

There are so many illiterates in our country, and most of the masses are ignorant. They don't know what "national products" are. The current problem of mass education is to improve the intelligence of the people and increase production. However, improving the intelligence of the people is never to guide them from the countryside to the city, from coarse cloth to Parisian silk, from dry tobacco pipes to British brands, and even foreign turbidity, foreign fire, foreign candles, foreign porcelain, foreign cloth and satin, foreign umbrellas... and all things foreign. If we improve the intelligence of the people in this way, the more the intelligence of the people is improved, the more dangerous the national products will be!

Under the current situation, how should the future mass education change its direction and implement "national product education"! It seems not very appropriate to take education as a method to solve the country's urgent and major problems. In fact, the educational facilities must be changed with the different needs of the times, and the greatest purpose of education is to enrich the country and strengthen the people, and promoting national products is the way to enrich the country!

A Humble Proposal on How National Product Industries Should Avoid Bad Debts

The current situation is so turbulent and unstable, and the social economy is so difficult and uneasy. They all stand still, let alone making progress. The lifeline of national products is becoming more and more urgent. This is really a very painful thing!

Because the customary practice of commercial changes is like this, if you want to promote your products far and near, you must extend credit to customers. If you want to do business, you have to ask people to prepare cash to buy your goods, which is impossible. In recent years, national product industries have been

Visiting Notes

A Visit to the Dahua Match Factory

It is truly shameful to say! Foreign goods flood our country, so much so that you can find them in any environment. Even on your own person, perhaps you can find quite a few! Yes, in today's China, where industry is undeveloped and real businesses are not thriving, if you were to examine the average citizen, you would find many foreign goods in their lives! In fact, you don't even need to ask them why they prefer foreign goods; it's not hard to imagine the reasons! The prices are too high, they feel the goods are inferior, or perhaps they've been buying them for so long that they're used to it. What is promoting domestic goods? That's what they would answer you!

As an intellectual myself, seeing my fellow countrymen favoring foreign goods, I do my best to persuade them to switch to domestic goods, but I can only feel sorrow in my heart. Even more sorrowful is that many intellectuals don't even consider the purchase of domestic versus foreign goods as a significant matter!

In my spare time from public duties, I considered visiting domestic goods factories. The goal was to plant the seeds of patriotism and support for domestic goods in the hearts of children. However, due to the burden of work and grading papers, I often wished to go, but was constrained by time. This time, because school had not yet started, I was introduced by my friends Mr. Mao and Mr. Shen, and was able to take the ferry to Liuliqiao in Pudong, Shanghai, and visit the Dahua Match Factory. I hereby record what I remembered during the visit:

The factory is located west of Liuliqiao, separated from Shanghai by only a river, and transportation is relatively convenient. Mr. Mao, Mr. Shen, and I walked to the gatehouse, and the gatekeeper immediately informed the inside. Before long, he brought out three passes and handed them to us. Led by Chief Chen Hanjian of the Engineering Department, we were able to visit all the facilities and observe the work inside the factory.

First, we went to the stem-sorting department, where countless messy match stems were piled up in the room. Two workers operated a machine, and another worker poured the messy stems onto it. Before long, they were all straightened. After the stems were straightened, several child laborers neatly placed them into square trays, presumably to take them out and put them into another machine to remove any that were uneven or unaligned! In one corner of the same room, two other workers managed two machines. Their job was to remove matchsticks with stems at both ends, as well as other oddly shaped matches! Mr. Chen said that the stem-sorting department is the first step in the match-making process.

Then we went to the second factory building, where there were many sections. Some removed stems that were too thick or thin, while others flattened stems in trays that were uneven in height. After the stems were arranged in trays, several workers coated the heads of the stems with a substance, in order to make the matches easier to light. Mr. Chen explained that this is why the match stems have distinct yellow and white sections! The wax tray was large and flat, and the oil simmered smoothly. The workers dipped the stems slightly, and they could be coated with phosphorus in a moment. The phosphorus was mixed with chemicals, and after the phosphorus was mixed by the machine, it was poured into a large machine pan to be ground finely. If this was not done, the finished matches would often have bursting or other defects. After the phosphorus was applied, they were taken to the drying department to be dried and boxed. In the drying room, there was a stove and a fan above it. Mr. Chen said that the purpose of installing the fan was to evenly distribute the heat from the stove around the room. In this way, the black heads of the matches would be beautiful and shiny. Otherwise, if the fan was not installed, the matches near the stove would often have black heads that were dry and stiff.

Later, we went to the boxing department, where we saw many female workers in two large rooms, all boxing matches. In the room, there was a path, with large boxes being packed on the left and small boxes on the right. The large boxes were branded "Horse" and sold well in the southeastern provinces of China, while the small boxes were branded "Cannon" and sold well in South and North China. When asked by Mr. Chen how many trademarks there were, he said there were many. From the boxing department to the packaging department, there were also many female workers who quickly wrapped ten boxes of matches into a bundle. I exclaimed in admiration. Mr. Chen replied, "Practice makes perfect. They are paid by the package, so the more they do, the more they earn." In another corner of the room, some workers used bamboo strips and bamboo hats to make large packages, so that when they were shipped to other places, they would not get wet like those packed in boxes!

The factory produces fifty or sixty large packages a day, totaling tens of thousands of boxes. The factory is also expanding greatly, adding factory buildings to expand production. The factory has a library, a fire brigade, a workers' night school, a sports ground, and a small garden. The workers' dormitories are also very clean. Labor and management have a harmonious relationship. The management strives for the happiness of the workers, and the workers also do their best to increase production! It is also worth noting that the factory's night school classroom is also the dining hall. The benches in the hall are square rings, with four wooden sticks inside the ring. When in use, a board is pressed on them!

Due to time constraints, I could not visit in detail, which I regret!

As competition increases, it becomes more and more fierce. In the struggle for dominance, everyone takes doing more business as a prerequisite, and has no time to consider the creditworthiness and economic status of customers. Most salespeople accept anyone who comes, and give out credit freely. By the time the payment is due, all kinds of difficulties arise, and bad debts are often heard of. I work for a domestic goods factory, and I have witnessed many such incidents. After careful consideration, I feel that in this situation, it seems necessary to try our best to come up with ways to remedy bad debts within the possible range. Therefore, I simply put forward the following naive views:

(A) Salespeople are responsible for reviewing. Salespeople in domestic goods factories should understand that they are not merely responsible for making a large number of sales. In fact, their task is not complete until the payment is received smoothly. Because the internal staff are not familiar with whether the customer's store is solid or whether their finances are comfortable, they rely on the salesperson's report as the basis for granting credit. If the salesperson does not have a careful eye and precise methods, it will greatly affect the security of the credit. In the past, it was customary in the business world to believe that salespeople did not need sufficient knowledge, and that it was enough to be able to sell the products. However, in today's complex social situation, where business conditions change rapidly, salespeople really should have knowledge and experience.

(B) Customer Economic Status Test Form. We often see many shops with a long history and good reputation suddenly close down and liquidate. In advance, it is indeed impossible to find a way to prevent it. But there is a very convenient way to remedy it in case of emergency, which is to create a systematic form for each customer that records the facts of their transactions over the years. The form should list the dates of delivery and payment, whether the payment is prompt, and the length of the promissory note. In this record, we can measure whether the customer's foundation is naive or strong, and how their economic status has changed. For example, if the dates of recent deliveries and payments are far apart, and the term of the promissory note is very long, then we must know that the customer is not as reliable as before, and we should consider it or urge them to pay the account. If there is no form to show it, and we only rely on vague ideas to estimate, it is very dangerous.

(C) Mutual Supervision of Business Among the Same Industry. At present, any industry is competing fiercely. Not to mention open and secret rebates, even the business area is very competitive. As a result, a situation of being indiscriminate and responding to every request is created. Since the same industry does not cooperate openly and honestly, there is even less talk of exchanging information. Therefore, I feel that the method of mutual supervision of business is really urgent. Because the same industry has an organization to supervise business, the general salespeople will have the opportunity to explore and ask questions of each other. The customer account will also have an additional procedure of brainstorming and detailed review, which will provide a little more guarantee for granting credit. Moreover, this organization can directly eliminate business competition, and everyone takes the same steps, which is a win-win situation.

I feel that the above three unsystematic contributions are very naive. Moreover, many bad debt incidents in the business world are caused by unexpected events. In fact, there is no secret to foreknowledge. Furthermore, if you want to expand your business, you have to give more customer credit. If you want to reduce losses, it seems better to give less customer credit. In this absolutely contradictory situation, salespeople who are engaged in the domestic goods industry really feel a lot of pain. I very much welcome everyone to discuss these kinds of issues, because these are the obligations that we comrades who are committed to domestic goods should fulfill!

Joint Business and Thorough Merger of Domestic Goods Enterprises

— Xun

Looking at the history of developing domestic goods enterprises, the reason why they are in a dying state and heading towards doom is that the dumping of foreign goods and poor management systems are certainly major reasons. In addition, the infighting and perennial struggles among the same industry, resulting in mutual harm, is also a fatal injury. Even if there are regulations that the same industry must follow on the surface, and there are indifferent associations, the competition of dreaming different dreams and acting independently becomes more intense. In the current year of constantly shouting about reducing labor, tightening budgets, and economic downturn, if there is no concrete way to give a shot in the arm, it is as dangerous as a patient with numerous external wounds and internal lung disease.

A few domestic goods enterprises that have already realized this have, in the past two or three years, created a joint business organization as if breaking through the siege. This organization is to establish a general distribution agency by connecting the same industry, and under the joint responsibility of the factory leaders, it achieves the effect of consistent business steps. From a practical point of view, we feel that the benefits that this organization contributes to an enterprise are indeed great, but from the perspective of overall cooperation, this is still a very one-sided and naive motive, and not a permanent destination.

Because simply uniting the business is not enough to unite the strength of an enterprise, and even more so because the concepts of interests in each factory cannot be eliminated, and there is still the idea of competing to be first, we dare to examine the joint business organizations of several domestic goods enterprises. It cannot completely recruit the participation of the same industry, and it fails soon after its creation, and many are fleeting. Only a few can obtain a thin lifeline and continue to work intermittently.

If the joint business is abolished because it cannot achieve the entire effect, and because the abolition restores the go-it-alone state of not being united, and the old state of competition among the same industry is revived, then there is no way to save it. We must understand that joint business at least has the advantage of brainstorming and taking steps in a disciplined manner. We must study this preliminary organization and take a further step to think of a thorough cooperation. How to be thorough? That is to follow the footsteps of European and American industries and implement the merger of the same industry.

In our country's industrial world, mergers of the same industry are rare, and it can be said that there are none. This is indeed a complicated and important matter. Each factory has its own fundamental position and internal asset share issues. When merging, there will inevitably be places where there are differences in weight. If you broaden your horizons and hope that there will be no competition in the future process and that it will flourish, then the money and time spent on the trouble during the preparation period is very worthwhile.

If the merger of the same industry is successful, not only will the business be unified, but there will also be advantages in product selection to learn from each other's strengths and make up for each other's weaknesses. The emerging industries are gradually assisted and merged, and the social recognition is also becoming more unified. In terms of resisting foreign goods, there is more abundant spirit and ability without worrying.

I believe that joint business is the foundation for mergers of the same industry. The organizations that have already joined the joint business should prepare quickly. All other industries that are in a smoky atmosphere should also pay close attention to it.

Contributing Opinions

A Careless Mistake

— Lantian

In this day and age, most gentlemen are making vigorous propaganda on promoting domestic goods in their speech and writing. They are truly enthusiastic patriots and can be said to be sparing no effort. However, very few of them have noticed that a very small and ordinary thing will make people more than ten years later have a vague impression and chaotic thoughts, and will not feel any pain or itch about domestic goods. What is this? Since the Chinese people were conquered by imperialism with force to open ports and trade, they have also used various economic policies to subdue us, so that our long-standing contemptuous psychology has turned into a psychology of worship. It seems that material civilization can only be created and invented by foreigners, and the Chinese people will never catch up. Therefore, whether this kind of goods comes from abroad and has been transformed by China itself, or is made by our own country, as long as it is novel and eye-catching, we do not distinguish right from wrong and collectively call it "foreign", such as soft yarn and cloth are called "foreign" yarn and "foreign" cloth, fine and clean thread and rope are called "foreign" thread and "foreign" head rope, cloth umbrellas for sunny days are called "foreign" umbrellas, enamel is called "foreign" porcelain, candles with wire cores are called "foreign" candles, small knives are called "foreign" knives, thread socks are called "foreign" socks, leather shoes are called "foreign" shoes, ... I can't write much here for a while. Although we know that they are domestic products, due to habitual laziness, we unconsciously blurt out the words, burying the domestic goods themselves at the bottom of the vast "foreign" sea.

It is no wonder that the general uneducated illiterates blurt out "foreign" and close their mouths with "foreign"! But those who are in the domestic goods industry and serve a small number of people, or the general primary school teachers who are entrusted with the mission of education to create the future masters of China, and the parents of the families, are also blindly following and shouting, isn't that too ridiculous?

Go Buy Domestic Goods!

— Huang Movei

In the mainland business world, domestic goods companies praise and sell all kinds of goods, and they are all complete.

The goods are so beautiful and the prices are so low! We go to buy things to eat, wear, and use, and we really feel: It is patriotic, economical, and cheap! Everyone go buy them quickly, go buy them from the "Domestic Goods General Warehouse"! The Japanese use peaches to teach children, explaining that peaches are produced in a certain place in China. The purpose is to suggest to children that they have a deep impression. If they do not seize the place that produces peaches, there is no hope of eating peaches and surviving. But how do the Chinese teach children? It is clear that this thing is a Chinese product, but it is made to be confused and inexplicable. Originally, many things were indeed introduced from foreign countries at first, but at present, there are many domestic goods invented or imitated by the Chinese themselves. So why "call a deer a horse" and still put the word "foreign" on it? Is it possible that only foreigners can make "foreign" goods, and Chinese people cannot make "domestic" goods? It is hoped that in the future, people who serve in the domestic goods industry, school teachers, and family parents must pay attention to this. If small things are neglected, it will have a bad impact on domestic goods, which is also creating a kind of shame for ourselves.

Domestic Goods Introduction

Two Things Worth Introducing

— Yu Youqing

Forgive me for being forgetful. I don't know which English novel said that a German, because of the stimulation of the people after the European War, suffered even more, so German expatriates in other countries became more enthusiastic about patriotism and promoted domestic goods. That German lived in England. One day, he ran out of cigarettes. For a while, he couldn't buy them from his home country. He walked all over London to buy German cigarettes. He searched for a long time. He finally managed to buy a pack of cigarettes that no one had asked about for a long time in a small grocery store. He was overjoyed and extremely happy. Later, he asked the owner of the small grocery store. He was also a German expatriate. His cigarettes were prepared for himself to smoke. When he saw someone coming to buy them, he was very surprised. He gave a pack of the cigarettes he often smoked to the buyer. Later, he made a good friend abroad. I won't say whether these facts are true or not. I think the Germans' patriotism and promotion of domestic goods are meticulous. Looking back at our Chinese people, they think that smoking foreign cigarettes is not enough to show off their wealth. They even want to smoke imported cigars! In comparison, the Chinese are too unpatriotic.

I also remember a friend saying that he had lived in Japan for more than ten years. He also held a position in a Japanese department store. When he met me, he often said that the Chinese are too unpatriotic. Japanese expatriates living in China use things that are all from their own country. Even for a toothbrush or a pack of toothpaste, they have to write a letter to their home country to buy it. This is how much they love to use domestic goods. But the Chinese are just the opposite. They think that if it is not an imported product, it is not enough to show that he is a modern person. He can't wait to learn everything from foreigners. It's a pity that his eyes are not green and his skin is not naturally white. Otherwise, he would definitely say that I am a European and American race. China is too undeveloped. From this point of view, Japan's strength is not an accident. You can know it by looking at the patriotism of the people. Chinese people, wake up.

Short Story

Marriage Change

— Xu Hongxia

The news of Hu Dazai's engagement to Ms. He Qin Fang was a surprise to his friends.

Indeed, from the point of view of all their circumstances, there was no possibility of engagement. Ms. He was a wealthy and powerful lady who had received a university education. Hu Dazai was a poor boy "without a tile to cover his head or a place to stand". The difference between the two was like "thirty-three heavens and eighteen levels of hell".

Ms. He originally had a lover, Dr. Wu Junren, who was a Japanese doctor of law and whose family was also very well-off. Friends were all sure that their marriage would not change.

A few days ago, Ms. He sent letters to Hu Dazai and Wu Junren, asking them each to send her a summer dress. Wu Junren received the letter and quickly ran to Company X to buy a pink-blooded silk cheongsam made of domestic goods and personally sent it to her.

Hu Dazai received the letter and suddenly realized his economic panic. He also felt that Ms. He was deliberately making things difficult for the poor. They had not been in contact for a long time, so why did she suddenly want a piece of clothing today? He touched his pocket and only had a dollar and a few cents left. Buying clothing was out of the question.

He thought about it and thought about it. He didn't even feel like eating dinner. He borrowed two dollars from a friend and ran to the XX Domestic Goods Company to buy a cheongsam material made of anti-Japanese yarn. He was embarrassed to send it himself, so he specially asked someone to send it to Ms. He. The next day, Wu Junren received a letter from Ms. He, which said:

"Mr. Junren:

Thank you very much for the summer dress you sent. After careful examination of the goods, they are actually enemy goods. Your purchase of these goods is helping the enemy to support their economy, buy bombs, kill our compatriots, and seize our land. Isn't the pink color a symbol of the blood of our compatriots? I can't bear to wear it, so I am sending it back to you. At this time of national crisis, you are still buying enemy goods. You are not a friend of mine. Please do not contact me again from now on! I wish you enlightenment. He Qinfang, August 10th"

So, the next day, He Qinfang personally ran to Hu Dazai's residence, on the one hand to thank him for his kindness, and on the other hand to seek his consent. That day, the engagement ceremony was held at the Qianghua Hotel.

Education News Foreign

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Education, Resigns

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Education, is physically weak and has suffered from insomnia and dizziness for a long time. After returning to Hangzhou from his hometown this time, his old illness could not be eradicated, so he decided to resign. Yesterday, he had prepared a memorial and submitted it to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education to resign from his concurrent positions as a member of the Provincial Government and the Director of the Department of Education. He also submitted it to the Provincial Government for transfer. Chen's resignation this time is extremely firm. He has ordered the departments to complete the closure and will leave Hangzhou for Shanghai to recuperate in a day or two. The affairs of the department will be temporarily handled by Secretary Qian Jiazhizhan. According to Chen, he told reporters that his intention to resign was decided as early as three months ago. The old problem of neurasthenia has been repeated from time to time, and he feels that his physical strength has not fully recovered. He does not want to hold a heavy task for a long time. However, at that time, the provincial games and qualifying examinations were waiting to be presided over, and the graduation examinations of this year, both senior and junior high schools, were held at the same time, which was the first time in this province. At the same time, the provincial finances were very tight. For the new educational facilities, patching up and repairing houses cost a lot of research, so he temporarily remained in office and planned everything. Now that the examinations have been completed, the educational budget has been determined, and the new schools that are being prepared have also been established. All schools have already started. At this time, the start of the academic year is the most appropriate time for transition, so he decided to resign. The central academy has already entrusted someone to Chen Jin, and he should be able to obtain approval. After approval, he plans to follow the doctor's advice and take a complete rest for six months or a year to cure his old neurasthenia and then decide on his future service policy.

Zhejiang Education Department Purchases Rare Song Dynasty Edition

Since the Song Dynasty, Zhejiang Province has been particularly renowned for its book collecting endeavors. The Fan Family’s Tianyi Pavilion was established during the late Ming Dynasty, while the Pinghua Studio, Zhenqi Hall, and Shousong Hall, among others, gained prominence in the early Qing Dynasty. Later, following the example of Anlu Lu’s Songlou and Qian Tang Ding’s Eight Thousand Scroll Building, they extensively acquired rare editions, earning widespread fame. Regrettably, the Lu family’s books soon flowed into Eastern Ying (Japan), and the Ding family’s books were also moved to Jinling (Nanjing). Few old families from the early Qing Dynasty remain, and renowned books and rare editions have been continuously flowing out of the province, leading to a decline in the book trade today, which knowledgeable people lament. The Sun family of Shousong Hall was a famous book-collecting family in Qian Tang during the early Qing Dynasty. Sun Yangzeng, the owner of the Siku Quanshu solicitation, once submitted a Song Dynasty edition of the "Collection of Inscriptions of Famous Song Dynasty Officials," which was recorded in the History section. Today, the Sun family has declined, and this book has survived numerous calamities. They wish to sell it to the government at a reasonable price. The collection, titled "Collection of Inscriptions of Famous Song Dynasty Officials," comprises 107 volumes in 32 books, written by Lin Dajiao of the Song Dynasty. It is an original engraving from the Shaoxi period of the Southern Song Dynasty, which was originally submitted during the Siku Quanshu solicitation and later returned. Subsequently, it was lost during the Taiping Rebellion and later recovered. During a fire that the Sun family experienced in the Republic Year Two, many fine books were destroyed, but this book happened to be in Shanghai and was spared. Now, the owner, Sun Kanghou, continues his ancestors' ambition and cherishes it deeply. However, Sun is devoted to learning and loves books but is unfamiliar with family management, leading to debt. Creditors intend to take the book as payment. Subsequently, prominent figures in the province, such as Wang Qianyang and Chen Qihui, fear that this precious book, which concerns the historical records of the province, will flow out of the province. They hope that the government will purchase it and preserve it within the province. The estimated value is three thousand yuan in national currency. The Zhejiang Provincial Library, inheriting the legacy of the Wenlan Pavilion, has a rich collection. However, good books outside the Siku Quanshu are mainly Ming Dynasty editions. It would be appropriate to seize the opportunity to collect them for public viewing. Therefore, they consulted with the library director, Chen Xun Ci. However, limited by a monthly budget of nine hundred yuan, even ordinary purchases are insufficient. They specially requested the provincial government to allocate a temporary book-buying fund of three thousand yuan for collection, to preserve it for the long term. The provincial government has already approved this proposal, and the Education Department is raising funds to order the purchase.

Municipal Library Preparing for Book Circulation

Also Planning to Expand the Library Site and Build Another Bookstore

The Shanghai Municipal Library is currently preparing for book circulation and plans to expand the library site and build another bookstore. Details are as follows:

Book Circulation

In order to increase the opportunity for citizens to read books and to utilize the function of books, the library has recently prepared a book circulation group. Those who wish to borrow circulating books must first fill out an application form at the library and submit a deposit. After review, a library card will be issued for borrowing books. When borrowing is no longer needed, the library card will be returned, and the deposit will be refunded upon presentation of the receipt. A delivery department will also be set up to hire people to deliver books to readers in distant areas, making it very convenient. Once approved by the Municipal Education Bureau, circulation will begin immediately.

Planning to Build a Bookstore

The library is located in the Confucius Temple Park, and the site is not very spacious. There are only a little over a hundred seats inside, but an average of two to three hundred citizens read inside every day, and there is already a shortage of seats. The books stored in the upstairs bookstore total more than 20,000 volumes, and the bookstore is full, leaving almost no space. If the number of books increases in the future, it will be impossible to accommodate them. Therefore, the library plans to submit a request to the Municipal Education Bureau to recover the public land behind the library in order to build a bookstore and add reading rooms, so as to provide convenience for readers. This plan is currently being drafted and will soon be realized.

Municipal Boy Scouts Actively Preparing for Shanghai Boy Scout Aircraft Naming Ceremony

The Municipal Boy Scout Council is preparing for the naming ceremony of the Shanghai Boy Scout aircraft. Yesterday, it ordered all Boy Scout groups in the city to proceed with the event on schedule. A Local Autonomy Experiment Village Centered on Elementary Schools

The Shanghai County Rural Improvement Association Approves Pilot Plan

Yao Huiquan, a member of the Shanghai County Rural Improvement Association, recently proposed a pilot plan for a local autonomy experiment village centered on elementary schools. The plan was approved by the second meeting of the association. Excerpts are as follows:

Location Selection The location of the experiment village should be selected according to the following principles: 1. There should be an elementary school principal and enthusiastic leaders trusted by the people. 2. There should be the ability to bear part of the expenses. 3. There should be concentrated villages. 4. There should be relatively convenient transportation facilities.

Preparations After the location is selected, a preparatory committee for the experiment village will be organized in conjunction with local people. The local elementary school principal and enthusiastic people will be designated to first visit places where village governance has been successfully implemented. The expenses will be borne by the association. Next, a detailed plan will be drafted and submitted to the county government for approval.

Administrative Organization The organization of the experiment village will follow the promulgated local autonomy laws and regulations. However, before the village head is elected by the people, he should be concurrently appointed by the county government as the principal of the local elementary school. The neighborhood chiefs and village chiefs will be selected by the village head and submitted to the county government for appointment. The village head will also appoint influential local figures as councilors to form a council. All actions will be supervised by the county government on one hand, guided by the association and the district office on the other, and accept the opinions of the local people on the other.

Funding The Funding should be in addition to the original elementary school expenses, a certain amount of money should be added for administrative expenses and a certain amount of money should be added for operating expenses. The monthly expenses should not exceed fifty yuan. The money will be shared by the county party headquarters, the county government, the district office, and the local area on average. Educational funding will be raised by the Education Bureau.

Experiment Period The duration of the experiment should be no more than three years. It must achieve the goals of popularizing education, increasing production, completing basic construction, establishing sound organizations, and electing village heads by the people. If it is found that there have been achievements after half a year or a year, it will be promoted to other places.

Chen Zhuzun's Opinion on the Facsimile Reproduction of Rare Siku Quanshu Editions

Recently, the Commercial Press and the Ministry of Education have discussed selecting and printing rare editions of the Siku Quanshu. Scholars at home and abroad have expressed many opinions. The reporter interviewed Professor Chen Zhuzun yesterday to ask for his opinion. Chen said that since it is named "Selecting and Printing Rare Editions of the Siku Quanshu," it should naturally be within the scope of the Siku Quanshu so that the world can see the true face of the Siku edition. If other ancient editions and good editions are selected to replace it, it should not be named "Siku." Moreover, the Commercial Press has previously reprinted the Sibu Congkan, Jigu Yicong, and issued the Hundred Na Edition of the Twenty-Four Histories. These books can be freely collected and published by scholars or merchants at home and abroad. Since they are not taken from official editions, there is no need to sign an agreement with the government or discuss them publicly. The reason for signing an agreement with the government and being subject to public discussion is precisely because it is taken from the Siku Quanshu, which is stored by the state. To abandon the Siku edition and not print it is to write an article outside the scope of the topic. As for making collation notes, it is also a matter for scholars to read books, not the responsibility of the printer. Besides, how many Ruan Wendas can be found today? If we must wait for the collation notes of each book to be completed before printing the books, I am afraid that the matter will never be completed. In my opinion, the most important thing in the facsimile reproduction of ancient books is to ensure that they are not distorted. Just like the facsimile reproduction of ancient paintings, even if there is damage or insect damage, no dots or strokes should be added arbitrarily. Therefore, even if there are wrong characters in the facsimile edition, they should not be changed, for fear that shallow people will mistakenly correct what is not wrong. Therefore, the first thing in the facsimile reproduction of ancient books is that there must be no intentional additions or alterations. The second is to prevent unintentional errors. Because the characters and strokes are not true when copying, they are often mistakenly changed when making plates. For example, the character 譌 (é) is mistaken for 共 (gòng), and the character 夫 (fū) is mistaken for 天 (tiān). This is something that we have to pay special attention to when making a facsimile. As for which books are rare and valuable, it depends on the selection of scholars, but scholars are not necessarily bibliophiles, and bibliophiles are not necessarily scholars. This is something that should also be known.

Past Overview and Future Facilities of Jinan University

President Zheng Reports at Reception for Faculty, Staff and Journalists

According to the school calendar, Jinan University began collecting fees and registering students on the 4th and is scheduled to start classes on the 11th. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. President Zheng Hongnian of the school held a tea party at the Hua An Building on the eighth floor of the Racecourse Hall at 3:00 PM yesterday to greet faculty, staff, and journalists from local newspapers on behalf of the students' parents. More than 100 people attended, and the school's staff, including Chen Qiying, welcomed them. At the designated time, the meeting began. During the meeting, President Zheng stood up to give a speech, first expressing his respect to the faculty and staff on behalf of the students' parents and welcoming the journalists from various newspapers to provide guidance and criticism on the school's various facilities. Next, he reported on the repairs and supplements to the various losses suffered by the school since the January 28th Incident, as well as the school's financial revenue and expenditure in the 21st year. He also reported on the implementation of the newly compiled curriculum in the 22nd year. The first year of the four years of university is for tool training, and the second year is for basic training. These two years are the early years of university, so that students from families with financial difficulties who cannot complete four academic years can be useful after leaving school. For those who study advanced knowledge, they can also find their own way. The third year is for professional training, and the fourth year is for experimental training. This is the later stage of the university, so that students who complete these four academic years can apply the knowledge they have acquired in the field. Finally, he explained the significance of overseas Chinese education and the special mission of the school. The guests and hosts parted happily at around 5 o'clock.

Shanghai Art College's Design Department Sets Up Free Tuition Slots

In order to promote production education and comply with the Ministry of Education's circular, the Shanghai Art College is working hard to implement practical art. Recently, it was learned that the school's president, Liu Haisu, believes that design is the mother of crafts, and to increase the productivity of crafts, design must first be popularized. Therefore, he plans to set up special free tuition slots in the design department starting this semester to encourage and seek opportunities for schools to have a practical connection with factories. The free methods are as follows: 1. The number of free tuition slots is temporarily set at eight. 2. The full tuition fee is waived, limited to the first semester upon admission. 3. Free students must be high school graduates or have equivalent qualifications and must be recommended by well-known factories or educational institutions with official letters. 4. Free students must pass the entrance examination. The examination date is from September 5th to September 20th and can be requested at any time.

The book prices are extremely modest.

靑光今日凱旋

Last night, they only won by one point against Qianghua, with a score of 36 to 35.

The Qianghua basketball team also lost to the Nanjing Qingguang team by a single point yesterday.

The score was thirty-five to thirty-six. It is unknown if the result would have been the opposite had Qianghua put Zha Wen-kui in earlier. It is noted that Qingguang has won all four matches in Shanghai, and their momentum is at its peak. Now that the competition is over, the team is scheduled to triumphantly return to Nanjing today. From beginning to end, the situation was unusually tense. After Qianghua took the lead with six to five, Qingguang's momentum suddenly turned, and they scored repeatedly, taking a sixteen to eight lead in the first half. All eight points scored by Qianghua were made by Cheng Jingxing alone. Starting in the second half, Qingguang's Wei Haiqing scored three consecutive baskets. Qianghua suffered this blow and tried hard to counterattack, showing great skill. The score gradually approached, leaping to twenty to twenty-two, with Qianghua only trailing by two points. The situation became increasingly tense, and the competition became more intense. Later, the score was once twenty-six to twenty-five, but Qianghua failed to overcome the one-point difference and remained at a disadvantage. Finally, when the score became thirty-five to thirty-six, Qingguang was penalized for their fourth timeout, giving Qianghua an unexpected advantage, thinking it would not be difficult to score the point and tie the game. However, Cheng Jingxing missed one, and Qingguang fortunately won by one point.

This performance was the toughest of Qingguang's four matches in Shanghai. Wei Haiqing of the team is a former famous Shanghai player, and his prestige has not diminished today. Xian Zhuanghuai is a famous Northeast player, and Li Chunfeng is an invaluable defensive pillar. Qianghua lacked sufficient practice, and their skills inevitably became rusty. Cheng Jingxing, Wu Youliang, and Xu Wenkui were the best in the team. It is a pity that Xu entered the game in the last ten minutes; otherwise, he could have helped Qianghua turn the tide. If the team can be given this day, there is great hope for them in the upcoming city games.

Essays

On a Young Couple's Suicide by Jumping into the Sea

— Zhanlu

Breaking the Modern Trend, Choosing a Clean Suicide

Everything has become modernized, and suicide is no exception. Swallowing raw opium and eating match heads have become outdated ways of committing suicide. The fashionable ghosts in the city of the dead mostly commit suicide by taking tranquilizer pills—that's modernized suicide.

Moreover, the places where they die are mostly hotels; the ways they die are mostly after "getting drunk and staying overnight" and "inviting others to play," returning to their rooms, sleeping, and never waking up again. "The deceased's belongings mostly include several suicide notes, one of which is an apology to the hotel owner; the deceased's photos and suicide notes can be published in newspapers, spreading the news for a while. If they die in inland hotels or places lacking news material, the local newspapers almost publish a special issue for the deceased, with everything extensively publicized. After a few days, all editorials and short essays in the newspapers use this as a modernized topic; this is the authority of modernized suicide.

Suicide is not what the brave do. Since they have already committed suicide and sacrificed their lives, what else can't they sacrifice? Why bother the hotel owner? Why occupy the newspaper's news space with rambling words? I read a Cantonese newspaper about a young couple's suicide on the Dragon Mountain Ferry and found it much cleaner than modernized suicides.

The Dragon Mountain Ferry departed from Guangzhou to Hong Kong. A young Chen couple in room 11 of the Western restaurant spoke the Chaozhou dialect. The man wore a thin woolen suit, and the woman wore a fashionable cheongsam. They had bought round-trip tickets the night before, going from Hong Kong to the province and then back from the province to Hong Kong. That evening at 7:00 PM, the two went to the dining room for a meal, which cost more than five yuan. After the meal, they returned to room 11. At 8:00 PM, a waiter from the Western restaurant entered the room to collect the bill but found no one there. The waiter assumed they had gone out for a walk and thought nothing of it. Around 9:00 PM, he entered the room again and still found no one. So he inspected the room and found a note saying: "I am not leaving a suicide note and will not say anything. Leaving five yuan is to pay for the meal. You can dispose of the other items." The handwriting was very neat. Among the belongings was a leather suitcase containing clothing and five yuan in Guangdong Provincial Bank notes. As for when the couple jumped into the sea, no one witnessed it. The passengers were just guessing. They went to the Qing stream together, without burdening others with their corpses, and left banknotes, just enough for the meal. There were no modernized suicide notes, only "Saying nothing." How tragic? How free? Suicide is not what the brave do, but this kind of suicide is much cleaner than modernized suicide after all.

Extraordinary Calm

— Yi

A few days ago, a very ordinary shooting case occurred in this city. A Ningbo native named Yu Agui was shot by an enemy. The detectives learned that the murderer was hiding in a house at No. 6 Huishan Road and secretly went to arrest him without making a sound. They found both the front and back doors of the house locked. When they broke in, they found no one inside, assuming that the murderer had escaped over the roof. Later, they discovered that he had jumped down from the kitchen shed and hid in the adjacent Lu Shunxing foundry. They went to the foundry and saw a Ningbo native named Xiang Xiasheng lying face down on the ground, his shoes covered in mud, which was quite suspicious. They asked the owner of the foundry, who said that he was not a worker there. So they took him to the police station. The police chief interrogated him, but Xiang resolutely denied it. When they took him to the hospital, the victim identified him as one of the murderers, and Xiang bowed his head without saying a word.

In Shanghai, this kind of case is too ordinary; it happens almost every day. But this murderer Xiang Zuisheng is very extraordinary, both alert and calm. The detectives went quietly, but he was able to jump down from the kitchen shed in advance and escape into the adjacent foundry, not only deceiving the detectives but also deceiving the owner of the foundry and many workers. When the detectives found out and went to the foundry, he was lying face down on the ground, and if it weren't for the "mud on his shoes," he would have deceived them again. This person's calmness is truly superior to alertness and can be called "extraordinary calm!" Because it is the instinct of bandits to want to escape when detectives come; as long as they escape quickly and hide well, that's enough. But lying on the ground and pretending to be asleep without revealing any flaws is very difficult. So although the case is ordinary, this person's calmness is extraordinary, and it is worth praising.

However, in today's China, calmness is extremely necessary. As a result of the advocacy of those above and the following of those below, calmness has become a habit. Bandits have their own personal needs, and this skill is even easier to practice to perfection. But even so, it feels like a desecration of calmness when bandits use it to deceive detectives. If the people of the whole country could practice it successfully and apply it to national affairs, that would make those above happy.

A Preface to the Flood

— Bibo

The rivers overflow, the waters rage, the cities are prosperous, all in vain, the sounds of a hundred sorrows break the heart, even chickens and dogs add to the misery, wandering and drifting are all prophecies, corpses float on the waves from time to time, a vast expanse of water becomes a swamp, angry waves pour into the divine land, rushing to rescue is too late, only to complain that the dikes were not repaired in peacetime. Even more so when the wind rages and the rain pours, wives and children are scattered and lost, the tragic situation is hard to describe, "even" a heart of iron would have tears "filling" their eyes, "the suffering people" suffer from frequent wars and foreign insults, climbing high to avoid disaster, few hills to shelter, in ancient times Dayu controlled the flood, passing his home three times without turning back, manual labor was not considered, benefiting the people and the country was the early plan, daring to hope that such a saint would be born in this world, but hoping that the donations would be rewarded, it is hateful that preventing the river "is difficult" than preventing the mouth, not first dredging the river "but" drawing the firewood from under the pot, the lives of the fish in the pond are attacked by disaster, who is the enemy who destroys their homes, who can restrain the raging waves that have already fallen, a long sigh does not pursue, "now is" the time to settle life and death, relief is urgently needed for clothing and food, "I urge my compatriots" to cherish kindness and help as much as they can, the scars are in my arms and I worry about people's worries,

If talking about cause and effect is too clichéd, "then talking about human love should also" be eager to rotate and not linger, "don't blame the storyteller" for chewing his tongue for no reason.

This opening has been broadcast on the Huadong Radio Station by the famous ballad singer Song Chen Ruilin.

Confucius Talks About Mahjong

— Pinshan

Zai Yu, Zi Huang, and Zi Xia are one player short. Purchased from Confucius. Confucius was pleased and said, "Mahjong is a small matter, but it has its merits. I have been talking about it for a long time. Even though you two or three gentlemen did not ask, I will still teach you." At the end of the game, Confucius won a great victory. Zi Gong asked, "Does mahjong also have a Dao? I am not clever. I wish to hear your teachings." Confucius said, "The Dao of mahjong can be summarized in one sentence: harmony is the most important thing, the small and the big depend on it, and knowing harmony and harmonizing should be done with etiquette. Therefore, a gentleman does not fight, but if he fights, he will surely win." Yan Yuan heard this and sighed, "The wisdom of the Master is truly unattainable!"

The Four Northeast Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Having a Family is Difficult, Hesitating and Worrying about the Future, Gathering with Friends and Shamefully Recalling the Past

Zhao Ziqiang just smiled and said in a low voice, "You said you wouldn't joke, you wouldn't joke, how come you're joking again?" Tian Qing smiled at Manying and said, "You're not sitting in the right place, come sit over here with me." As he spoke, he patted a square stool next to him repeatedly with his hand. Manying glanced at the people and said, "Are you making fun of me, or what?" Zhao Ziqiang also laughed and said, "Look, even Ms. Huang is unhappy with you." Manying stood up and said, "If you say that, I'm going to sit over there, see what happens?" Guizhi quickly grabbed Manying's clothes and laughed, "Why move when you're sitting so well?" Manying said, "Ms. Yang, are you being reasonable or not?" Guizhi said, "How am I being unreasonable?" Manying said, "Since you're being reasonable, I can sit wherever I want, that's my freedom, why are you interfering with me?" As she said this, she remained standing, unwilling to sit down. Guizhi threw up her hands and said, "If you want to move, then move, I'm not afraid." Manying wasn't afraid of him getting angry. She moved her cup of hot cocoa to the other side first, and then she sat over there herself. Guizhi lowered her head but glared at her with the corner of her eye. Manying didn't mind at all and smiled slightly. Tian Qing nudged Zhao Ziqiang and said, "Old Zhao! Say something!" Zhao Ziqiang took out a handkerchief from his pocket and kept wiping the sweat from his forehead. Tian Qing sighed and said, "You're really useless!" Zhao Ziqiang said in a low voice, "Don't joke around." Tian Qing said, "Even if you can't talk, can't you even entertain guests? Come, come, let me entertain them for you first." Just then, the waiter brought in several bowls of yuanxiao and placed them on one end of the table. (180)

Whereabouts

Rural Life in Jiangwan

— Hu Juju

Having idled away many years, this past Sunday was finally the most memorable. We should thank Zhou Shixun, the “Happy Immortal,” for bestowing this kind of outing upon us, which might even prolong our lives.

Speaking of Shixun, among our friends, he is recognized as the happiest. He has two nicknames that suit the seasons: in winter, he’s called "Café Owner," and in summer, "Yuyuan Road Inspector." From these two elegant titles, one can see a general picture of his life. The most troublesome thing about him is his oily mouth, which never stops moving for a minute, except when he's asleep. But when he does speak, every word he utters makes everyone burst into laughter. Therefore, I added the title "Tiger's Mouth" to his oily mouth. In public conversations, it's difficult for anyone to escape his "Tiger's Mouth." Because of his “happiness” and talkativeness, friends always remember Shixun when planning outings. Without him, it would be dull and uninteresting.

Recently, his life has undergone a small change. He has shifted from "urban" to "rural." "Zhapu," "Jiangwan," or "Gaoqiao" and "Donggou" have all been unceremoniously regarded by him as his own paradise, proclaiming himself as one of the part-owners.

Last Sunday, he made an appointment with me in advance, along with Shen Hengzhuang and Zhang Qiuxin, deciding to spend this Sunday in rural life. On that day, early in the morning, the three of us were "expelled" from the city by Shixun with gentle persuasion, walking along the Jiangwan Road, faintly marked with bloodstains, to Jiangwan. We were extremely tired along the way, but fortunately, among the four of us, we had this "pocket-sized" golden tongue, so we didn't feel bored.

Arriving in Jiangwan, we rested our feet at Wanxiangpu, which is the garden of Mr. Wang Zhongheng, Shixun's father-in-law. Although the land is not very vast, with several acres of fertile fields and a thatched cottage, it felt quiet and peaceful, at least isolated from the noise of the city. Moreover, the garden is adorned with chickens and dogs, fully revealing the flavor of rural life. At this time, compared to the farmers and villagers, the four of us felt our own worldliness. So Shixun ordered everyone to shed their worldly clothes, and at the same time, everyone took up their respective farming tools, putting away their armor and returning to the fields, trying out the life of farming. It was probably just a one-time thing, but we felt extremely happy.

After working, the gardener, Xiaomao, brought up a large amount of cooked corn. We also gathered fallen flowers together, spreading them on the grass and sitting on them. Shixun said, "This is a flower carpet," which was very elegant. Qiuxin loved eating vegetables and fruits the most, and Qiuxin ate half of the total amount of corn from the large plate.

After finishing the meal, led by Xiaomao, we brought our own pre-Qingming tea and went to a small teahouse in the town to drink tea. This teahouse is called "Jiangyuan," and it is the leading tea garden in Jiangwan. The exterior is extremely ugly, but inside, there is an elegant room, which is a gathering place for the local gentry. Because of the timing not conflicting, we were honored to be guests. Shen Hengzhuang liked to drink, and suddenly he had the urge to have beer, entrusting Xiaomao to get it for him. As a result, after an hour of searching, there was only one bottle in the whole town. So Qiuxin and I withdrew, and Shixun and Hengzhuang drank together. The two of us borrowed a set of chess pieces to play chess. Unfortunately, the two of us didn't have beards, otherwise we would have stroked them as we walked, which would have been truly antique. After finishing the wine and the chess game, it was evening. The little sparrows had already gathered in pairs and returned to their nests. We were not yet satisfied, so we went back to the garden and picked some purple grapes to quench our thirst, eating almost all the grapes on one trellis before we felt refreshed. Then we prepared to return to the city. Before leaving, Shixun borrowed flowers to present to each person a pot of autumn colors. This was originally a good thing, but strangely, the purple-orchid colored leaves had green edges. Shixun said, "This country girl has been infected with urban modernity," which was also quite interesting.

Returning to the North Station, it was past seven o'clock. We parted ways and hurried home. Although this was a small separation from our wives, it suddenly reminded us of the loneliness of the women at home. So everyone returned like an arrow, without discussion, getting on two-wheeled vehicles and heading home, far away from the countryside.
