Free Talk

Throwing Stinky Stuff

— Xu Mao

After reading Mr. Dafu's "Biographical Literature," I want to talk about another kind of "biography" 丨丨 but not "literature." Looking at the current market, besides those "self-singing and self-praising autobiographies and plagiarized critical biographies," there are also popular texts such as anecdotes and secret records. These authors often capture facts that are only shadows of reality, or fabricate rumors that have no basis at all, using human curiosity and claiming to have secret knowledge, so they often win a large readership. The origin of this school of thought comes from previous unofficial histories. A group of old-fashioned literati in Shanghai used it extensively, not only as a source of conversation after tea and wine, but also as a means of coercion and slander. Now, a group of new-style literati in Shanghai are using it even more sharply as a tool to achieve certain goals. Therefore, although this is not "literature," it does have the flavor of "the art of weaponry."

Saying it's a weapon is actually still not right, because if it were a weapon, then one side should be Huyan Zhuo's chain horses, and the other side should be Xu Ning's hooked sickle spears; one side should be the Jin people's wolf-toothed clubs, and the other side should be the Song people's heavenly spirit caps. But now it's not like that. People are originally unarmed, and since you can't add any charges to them, but you want to attack them, what should you do? You can only "throw stinky stuff."

The two methods of revealing private matters or fabricating rumors are what the people of Shaoxing call "throwing stinky stuff." "Liao" means fertilizer.

Throwing fertilizer on the enemy makes third parties hate the enemy's stench. This is exactly the same as the ingenuity of the manufacturers of current anecdotes and secret records.

A brave warrior with extraordinary courage can still risk his life to resist for a while when encountering a hooked sickle spear or a wolf-toothed club, even if he is empty-handed. But if the opponent uses "stinky stuff," then no matter how brave he is, he can only quietly retreat. It is not surprising that the "stinky stuff" literati can be proud for a while.

From "Place to Use One's Talents" to "Environment"

— Suo Yuan

After reading Mr. Qian Gechuan's article the day before yesterday, I deeply sympathize with the distress of Mr. Qian and others, who feel that "the environment does not allow us to completely abandon English" and "have to" do the "85 Movement." Therefore, I regret my meddling. If Mr. Qian and others had declared their "environment" earlier, I would never have dared to criticize them rashly. But since I have received a reply, and before the "scholars of the whole country" come to "answer on behalf of" Mr. Qian and others, I have to talk to Mr. Qian again.

The predecessors point out two very important points in Mr. Qian's article: ㈠ Basic English is not an international language. Zhang Menglin's "English 85 Movement and Basic English," two. The words of the originator Ogden quoted therein, three. Basic English's "Introduction" and "Grammar" two books, as well as the advertisements for Basic English published in various magazines and newspapers, all declare that Basic English is an international language. But now Mr. Qian declares that Basic English is only "seeking a simple shortcut within the scope of English." Because it is a "shortcut" "within the scope of English," it is definitely not a rationalization plan for English that can stand side by side with English and replace it, let alone be a higher-level (level in the development stage of language) international language. It is already very obvious. So it is just a kind of English learning method, or "shortcut," that is inseparable from the original English.

(Two) "Each has its strengths and weaknesses, each has its own field." In Mr. Zhang Menglin's article, the crimes of Esperanto have been determined: one. It is "artificial, a dead thing," two. Learning it "is equal to learning another foreign language," three. "Moreover, it has no motherland, that is, even if you learn it, there is no place to use your talents," "so it cannot be called upon." But now Mr. Qian declares: "Esperanto and English each have their strengths and weaknesses, each has its own field," "I have not opposed Esperanto because I have learned English." Here, Mr. Qian has confirmed the existence of Esperanto, expressing "not" "opposing" it, and believes that the two are "not only non-invasive to each other, but also can be learned concurrently."

In general, I agree with the above two points. Below, I will list a few points that I cannot agree with and answer them:

㈠ Mr. Qian said: "I think Esperanto comrades will certainly not attack English because they have learned Esperanto." My reply: In my articles and the articles criticizing Basic English that I have read (The Analects, Tao Sheng, Peiping World Daily, Shanghai Morning Post), no one has ever made half a word of attack on English itself. What I oppose is: one. Basic English that attempts to be an international language ("motherland" "place to use one's talents"), two. Basic English that attempts to be a rationalization plan for English ("English Rationalization and Basic English"). Mr. Qian used the method of "switching packages" and entangled with me. But he did not answer the main points of my argument. It is said that because "there are facts that can prove it," so "I am unwilling" to "talk empty talk on paper."

(Two) Mr. Qian quoted my "I can't help but say it is a complete failure," attempting to imply how arbitrary I am. In fact, my original text is not as simple as quoted. I said that if Basic English is not regarded as a kind of English learning method that is inseparable from English, but attempts to be a rationalization method that can replace English, "I can't help but say it is a complete failure." And Mr. Qian also admits that it is only a "shortcut" "within the scope of English" and does not act as a language that can be independent from English. So this "complete failure" "has facts that can prove it," and there is no need for "scholars of the whole country" to "answer on behalf of" again.

㈢ Regarding the rationalization of English spelling, Mr. Qian, in addition to "hoping" that I "study on my own" why the Americans do it, recited a history from the "sixteenth century." In terms of spelling rationalization, Anglic is better than Basic English, needless to say. Mr. Qian did not delve into the rationalization of spelling itself, only saying that it "does not help much" hastily. My reply: Mr. Qian, let's talk about Basic English first. Anglic, why the Americans do it, let's talk about it later!

㈣ Regarding the rationalization of irregular verbs and the exceptions of most nouns, Mr. Qian is affirmative. "But besides artificial languages, what kind of living language is completely rational?" My reply: The failure of Basic English as a rationalization plan for English lies in its failure to artificially and consciously control the existing language. But to have Ogden create such a plan is as impossible as having Dr. Hu Shi join the volunteer army. For more than ten years, Chinese opponents of Esperanto, from Mr. Tao Menghe of the "New Youth" era to Mr. Zhang Menglin and others now, have no theory other than a few sentences they have heard: "artificial language," "dead thing," "newly created world language."

It's really shallow.

㈤ Mr. Qian finally said: "Does learning a country's language make us citizens of that country?" Naturally, learning English will not cause the skin to turn white or the hair to turn yellow, just as eating beef will not turn you into a cow. However, it also depends on the "environment." If under the power of "dollars," "gold pounds," and "the saber of the imperial army," the "environment" "does not allow" you to not engage in such language movements, it is indeed the most vicious weapon of enslavement and colonization. Therefore, Mr. Qian's words, besides intentionally or unintentionally defending the forced learning of Japanese in "Manchukuo," have no other meaning.

The Ideal Characters of Writers (Continued)

— Shi Heng

What are the characteristics of Sanin? First, Sanin has an extraordinary and astonishing discourse on sexual desire; second, he is extremely opposed to knowledge; third, he has an extremely strong physique. These points are precisely the keys that most of the Russian intellectual class in the 1880s were most troubled by. In the works of Artzybasheff, we can clearly see that he is a member of this troubled intellectual class. His troubles, 丨丨 the troubles of himself or people of the same class, resulted in him fantasizing about this freak Sanin, and even more exaggeratedly expressing it in art. This kind of fantasy is the same as the British writer Stevenson, who suffered from chronic lung disease throughout his life, excessively praising the state of health.

However, Artzybasheff did not succeed in the expression of his ideal character Sanin, because he lacked too much authenticity, and it was almost impossible to make people believe that it was possible to exist. Sanin, with his extraordinary explanation of sexual desire, and then as a practical proof of the theory of seducing and provoking beautiful daughters or even carnally embracing his own sister, how despicable this should be; with his antipathy to knowledge, 丨 only a moment on five hundred pages of books mentioned that he was reading, and then confirming his spirit or talkativeness, how romantic this should be; with his display of stupid physical strength, he then produced a special pair of characters to change him from being beaten with a whip to being protected by wooden oars, how meaningless this should be; even that the ending of the whole family, which many people take as a good story 丨 Sanin bravely jumped out of the train to exhale because he hated the faces of human beings on the train, how absurd this scene should be.

In short, Sanin is a character created in fantasy, stemming from the author's long-term suffering from his own shortcomings, and intentionally exaggerating what he considers to be an ideal character, and this character is beyond all possibilities of realization. If such a contrived thing has undergone a complete and refined artistic rendering, it may also become a typical character, deceiving later readers as a character that once actually existed (there are countless such examples in the history of literature), but unfortunately Artzybasheff's art has failed to achieve this step, and we can see his intentional contrivance everywhere.

From the example of Sanin, our authors can be offered a lesson, that is, it is extremely unlikely that all authors' conceptual or delusional characters will want to deceive readers into accepting them as a typical character.

(Note: 丨 The words of Volovscky quoted in the text are based on the translation of Mr. Studio, with one or two words added or subtracted.) (End)

Seaside Night

— Bing Xin

In black clothes, the three of them walked on the soft, loose sand.

Each with different feelings, quietly walking towards the seaside 丨 the seaside with lights, the wind is not very strong, but blowing on them who have just run out of the hot like a sauna cabin, there is simply unspeakable coolness and comfort.

A new crescent moon had just climbed out of the seabed in the east, and the light was so faint that it was impossible to see the color, if it wasn't for the moon shadows and wave light rippling in the sea that they saw.

Gradually approaching the shallow beach near the sea, this is the beach that has just been washed by the tide, softer and wetter than the one they had just walked on. The wind blew in gusts, and the sound of the tide hitting the rocks and crashing on the beach was so loud and majestic that it made them shout out;

Chen straightened her chest and shouted loudly, Zhu stared at the sea and kept saying, "It's great, it's great!" Xin, like a little sparrow, jumped and sang the song Moon night.

They were so happy, like prisoners sentenced to life imprisonment suddenly escaping from prison, all the troubles and heat were gone, just throwing themselves into the embrace of nature without any worries. They didn't care about each other, just stepping forward step by step on the soft, cotton-like fine sand.

The entire universe was immersed in silence, and if there were no wind and the sound of the sea tides, you would simply suspect that you had entered the land of the dead and that you had become a ghost.

"Let's not go too far, let's just sit here and watch the sea," I don't know if Zhu was tired from walking, or if she didn't have the courage to walk in the dark, she stopped alone. (To be continued)

Woman (14)

— Shen Congwen

What about the boy? He liked her. When he was in front of her, he was lively and young. When he left her, he had no interest in anything. His heart was in turmoil. He still didn't know how to say "he loved her" to her. He didn't understand what love was.

She understood that he wouldn't know how to explain the love that was troubling him in his heart. She felt that the beauty in these aspects always formed a five-colored rainbow in her heart.

But the two became friends by chance, but they still had a misunderstanding by another chance, and finally they separated. (A very long winter.)

That autumn, he transferred to the science department of X University in Beijing, and she also went to Beijing and entered the second grade of the liberal arts department of XX Church University.

They still met. She became a seventeen-year-old girl he had seen on the coast of the South China Sea, and she had to have that boy.

She loved him. But because he understood that she was a daughter of an official, and from some unsubstantiated rumors, he learned some stories about this woman, he avoided her as much as possible.

Age also formed a barrier between the two. The woman became a person who had been jilted unexpectedly. In all kinds of indifference, she still maintained her sincerity. As for him, he was just a twenty-one-year-old boy with a strong temperament and too much simplicity. He only wanted to have an achievement in chemistry in the future and make a contribution to the country. This simplicity made him see love differently from ordinary men. In fact, he was still a child. Once he had faith, he didn't want love.

So, in a pile of unremarkable consecutive days, nearly a thousand days passed. The two lived very self-respectingly in a close friendship.

In the end, they finally broke up. The woman had already graduated and spent a year in the graduate school of that school, and he had also graduated. She understood that this matter should have a result, so she ended this matter and told him that she was preparing to go to France. The man just used the attitude he had become accustomed to in the past three years to express his agreement with what she said. He later told her that he only wanted to work as an assistant technician in an acid factory in Shanghai, save money, and then go abroad to study.

She told him that as long as he wanted to study, she was willing to treat him as a good friend and let her lend him some money. He said that he didn't want to study like this. This kind of studying was meaningless.

They said other things, and this proud and beautiful man almost completely answered the woman in the same tone.

After that, she didn't say anything and just prepared to leave.

He happened to be poisoned in the laboratory at this time.

Later, he was admitted to the hospital and became a permanent resident in the ward of XX Hospital. The small chair next to the patient's bed in the ward was often occupied by that woman.

People's temperaments are always gentler when they are sick.

Every day, they reviewed everything on the sea three years ago. This sea in each person's impression was brightly colored, but when the two looked at each other, they were not as innocent as before. This disease gave the woman many opportunities, so that the woman's tenderness, in various small matters, made the patient lying in the white sheets understand it and understand it.

(Spring, a spring with melting snow. No, the yellow leaves testify, this is not spring!)

Commercial News

Gold, Commodity Prices, and Stocks Decline; Premium Rises Ten Yuan and Seven Cents

丨 Continuing to fluctuate in a narrow range 丨

The gold market rebounded again yesterday, with a stable trend, but the fluctuation range was still narrow. In the morning, although the London spot and New York silver prices rose slightly, the British-American exchange rate narrowed by 1.75 points, the American-British exchange rate increased by 2.25 points, and the futures silver prices on the Five Metals Exchange increased by 0.38 cents and 0.32 cents respectively. Private Estimates of American Cotton

New York, 5th. The Barnwell Publishing Office announced its estimate for the new cotton crop this year. The harvest condition is 64.4% of the normal year, and the cotton field is 31,535,000 acres. The previous estimate (July 4) was 74.1% of the normal year, the cotton field was 40,645,000 acres, and the harvest yield was 13,760,000 bales.

Views of Flour and Wheat Industry Insiders

Yesterday's newspaper reported that the relevant departments of the Central Government held a meeting on five items to maintain the wheat law. Although the details are not fully known, the morale of the city was boosted and the wheat price was pushed forward. However, according to industry insiders speaking from facts, the wheat had already been purchased, and the international telegrams were undoubtedly confirmed. At present, they are considering how to find a way out and how to distribute it to Chinese merchant factories at what market value. As for the sluggish flour sales this year, it is no accident. The main reason is the economic bankruptcy in various places. Recently, the accumulated flour in Tianjin is still slightly less than 3 million bags, and there are also 3 million bags in this city. The wheat stored in each factory can last for at least two months. Even with this amount and the actual sales in recent years, it is enough for half a year. If the wheat production in various places is included, even if foreign wheat is not scheduled, it can last until the new wheat season next year. Therefore, no matter how to provide relief, it will not be possible to escape the facts and find another way out. Because China's economic downturn is no different from the surplus overseas. It is difficult for countries with gold and yuan to break through this difficulty. Does our country have the power?

Each European bank urgently needs to sort, pack, and transport the large amount of Zhenmei and Xiamei green tea purchased a few days ago for export. Therefore, they have temporarily stopped purchasing various teas in the market. Only Hua Tea, Xiehe, and other firms in the city purchased more than 900 boxes of green tea such as Zhenmei and Zhenmei, and the selling price did not change. In addition, the Tongfu Foreign Bank has slightly improved its interest in Qimen black tea, and the selling price has not risen or fallen.

Hardware, Cement, and Steel Transactions are Launched

The golden wind is refreshing, and the source has disappeared. The hardware market is also gradually becoming active. Various manufacturers have begun to contact each other in preparation for winter goods. It is estimated that 2,000 boxes of tinplate and Huisai iron have been ordered, and the market is better than before. It is estimated that 90 pounds per box is 16.4 yuan, 100 pounds is 17.2 yuan, and Huisai iron is 32 yuan. 18-sheet chimney iron, then the North gang bought 500 loads, priced at 11.25 yuan, 0.2 yuan less than before. English steel plate 2.5 mm is 10.05 yuan, 200 loads are opened, and 0.5 mm is 8.5 yuan, and only a hundred loads are traded. 7.5 mm is only a few dozen loads, and the buying and selling market has not changed. The Fujian gang loaded 4 or 500 barrels of Elephant brand cement, priced at 4.7 yuan per bag and 5.85 yuan per barrel (including tax). There are only a few transactions in this factory's nails, and the market is stable. In addition, various iron products are expected to develop in this cool weather.

Business Sutra (39)

The Effects and Uses of Ginkgo

Summer has passed, and cool autumn has arrived. Streets and alleys are filled with a chorus of cries, resounding in the ears: "Hot ginkgo nuts, fragrant and glutinous!" This is the cry of vendors selling so-called "hot ginkgo," a very common seasonal treat in Shanghai.

Ginkgo refers to the kernel of the fruit produced by the ginkgo tree. The ginkgo, also known as the "grandfather-grandson tree," is a deciduous tree, five or six fathoms tall, with thin, fan-shaped leaves that have notches. In spring, it bears small, white flowers with a hint of light green. It bears fruit in early autumn. The flesh is removed to obtain the kernel, which is the ginkgo nut.

The naming of ginkgo is based on its inherent shape and color. When the kernel is fresh and tender, it is bright and green. After some time, it takes on a yellowish hue. It is oval in shape, with small, pointed ends, resembling an olive, but with ridges. It may have two or three ridges. Those that meet this standard are called "Buddha's Hand Fruit" and are of the highest quality. There are also those that are round, like cherries, called "Plum Fruit," which are of a relatively lower quality.

Ginkgo is sweet and bitter, neutral and astringent, and non-toxic. Cooked, it has the effect of warming the lungs and benefiting qi. The Compendium of Materia Medica has several applications for it. I will extract one or two as follows: (1) For facial rosacea and chapped hands and feet, chew raw ginkgo and apply the juice. (2) For frequent urination, eat fourteen ginkgo nuts, half raw and half roasted. (3) For leucorrhea, grind ten raw ginkgo nuts, mix with warm water, and swallow once a day. This is very effective. (4) For breast lumps that have ulcerated, grind half a catty (eight ounces) of ginkgo nuts, mix with wine, and drink. Grind the other half catty (eight ounces), apply as a poultice. This is effective.

Another Interpretation of "Poverty," "Stealing," and "Robbing"

— Qian Xu

丨Written after reading Mr. Yin's "Stealing" and "Robbing"丨 "Stealing and robbing" are not "human" "instincts," but "poverty" can indeed "ignite passionate and upward-moving emotions." This was stated very clearly and thoroughly in Mr. Yin's article "Stealing and Robbing" in this journal on August 31, 1933. In the end, it even strongly cited "World Revolutionary Literary Giant Gorky" as hard evidence. Originally, I could have "remained silent" about this. The reason I didn't "remain silent" is that I still felt there were a few "different points," and the purpose is to hopefully reach more, and at the same time, more thorough and clear conclusions. Therefore, the writing of this article is definitely not an intentional attack or meaningless rebuttal.

"Suicide" is the act of "the weak," and I absolutely "do not deny" this. However, I cannot "despise" it like Mr. Yin because I believe this is the inevitable result of the deformed development of society. At the same time, it is also a helpless and "tragic" way to "escape" from "poverty." Therefore, I only feel sympathy and regret for these many victims and try my best to provide relief and active assistance to reduce this "tragic" phenomenon. Eight or nine out of ten reasons for "suicide" are because of "poverty," and "poverty" has now almost become a "universal disease"! In Mr. Yin's view, "poor people" must "endure hardship," and only after going through the stage of "poverty" can they achieve "permanent, great, and genuine creation." There seems to be a similar saying in our ancient proverbs: "Endure the bitterness of bitterness to become a man above men." However, the reality tells us that many people who have lived a life of "hardship" in peace and poverty still fail to become "men above men"! Therefore, I cannot help but feel suspicious about "poverty." Now, I am even more suspicious of whether "World Revolutionary Literary Giant Gorky," who "survived countless struggles in the waves of poverty and finally succeeded," is just one of the lucky few among millions of "poor people"?

As for "robbing" and "stealing," my understanding is not as narrow as Mr. Yin's. Because if someone truly becomes a thief or robber due to "poverty" to "steal" or "rob," then not only is there "no hope of warmth, food, and enjoyment," but also, because this is a criminal act, there is the danger of "detention," "imprisonment," and even being "shot." This is the act of a "poor wretch" and should be "punished."

My so-called "stealing" and "robbing" are actually the principles of struggle, progress, practical, and creation that Mr. Yin speaks of. "Stealing" is other people's methods, like the Japanese's ability to imitate and copy... "Robbing" is other people's interests, like capitalist countries plundering the possessions of small and weak nations. Such "stealing" and "robbing" can be as big as possible because only broad and planned "stealing" and "robbing" can be a "raging fire," can "ignite passionate and upward-moving emotions," and can further become "permanent, great, and genuine creation," which is the true way out for "poor people." Therefore, I firmly believe that "stealing" and "robbing" are "human" "instincts."

Autumn Brings Sorrow

— Wei Ren

On an autumn evening, August 30th, the half-moon was slowly climbing up the eastern grape trellis. The rustling leaves of the parasol tree were constantly struck by the wind, falling to the ground, and from the grass pile at the foot of the wall, autumn insects were singing a tragic battle song as if they were going mad. On a thin layer of withered yellow and slightly red parasol leaves, the moonlight reflected two closely intertwined slender figures. At the same time, in the still air, weak, subtle conversations drifted from the grape trellis.

"Sister Ling, I'm leaving for sure tomorrow. I have to leave her. But..." I turned my back to her face, feeling so sad that I almost shed tears as I spoke to her.

"Younger brother Hui, parting may be the most painful thing, but for the sake of everything for you, you should still go! I believe the world won't be as cruel as you imagine. You can find someone to comfort you anywhere. Besides, your mission is calling you to reach out to all the people in the world!" She turned my head around like a loving mother and said kindly.

Her kindness and dignity made me believe in her sublimity and greatness even more. We talked intimately under the bright moonlight. We talked about our past, present, and future. When I thought of the uncertain wandering in the future, I felt lost. I said:

"Sister Ling, how will I struggle in an environment that I have never lived in before?"

"Younger brother Hui, why are you so worried? You will know how important your lifelong responsibility is! So, what does our temporary separation count for?"

"..."

"What, are you crying? This is a trick played by idle women! Don't be silly anymore. Lift your head up and show some courage, younger brother Hui!" We talked and talked until the autumn night wind brought a chill.

This was an autumn night of parting last year. But how quickly time flies! Drifting in S Province...
